mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">程玉兰</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、程渊</span><b mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">崔太、</span><span minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">蔡葆菊</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：辽宁沈阳市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1963</span>年生，，沈阳市浑南新区桃仙镇人。蔡葆菊<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日遭警察抓捕、抄家；<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日她被浑南分局正式逮捕，后获悉她被沈阳经济开发区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，并被罚金一万元，现在她被关押于沈阳第一看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/10/5.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">蔡彩影：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广东佛山市张槎小学英语教师、法轮功学员。蔡彩影在中共<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月迫害法轮功以来，她曾多次被绑架迫害，曾经被非法判刑七年，家庭破碎。蔡彩影<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月被抓捕，被关押在佛山看守所，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月左右，蔡彩影被佛山市禅城区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，目前被关押在广东省女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">蔡华兴：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">广州市白云区法轮功学员。广东省茂名市电白区马踏镇长山湾塘村人，<span lang="EN-US">1980</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月出生。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，中共发动对法轮功的迫害时，蔡华兴还不到十九岁。在中共对法轮功二十多年的迫害中，他因坚持修炼法轮功，曾被劳教和关洗脑班迫害。曾遭吊铐和毒打，致使他说话困难。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日晚上，蔡华兴放了一份法轮功资料，遭恶告。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，蔡华兴在住处被白云区公安分局国保警察和均禾派出所警察抓捕，关进白云区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被广州市荔湾区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，被罚金一万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/14/458791.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/14/458791.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">蔡林华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">广东揭阳市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，广东揭阳市揭西县法轮功学员吴春雄在揭阳榕城区新河村自己的公司被揭阳市公安局东升派出所抓捕，公司的几名员工吴旭钦等也被抓捕。据悉，是公司的微信公众号出现有法轮功的真相。随后，派出所人员胁迫吴旭钦带他们到家里非法抄家，并抓捕了吴旭钦的母亲陈晓彬，还用封条把家门都封了。吴春雄原本生意很好的公司全面停运，同时很多私人物品被非法抄走。吴春雄、吴旭钦、陈晓彬、蔡林华等被关押在看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月上旬，广东揭阳市榕城区法院在揭阳市判法轮功学员蔡林华<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">蔡伟华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，哈尔滨市法轮功学员。大学本科毕业，从事财务统计工作多年。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日过遭抓捕，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月初，蔡伟华被入黑龙江省女子监狱迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">蔡秀瑛：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黑龙江</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">哈尔滨市香坊区法轮功学员，其丈夫原是哈尔滨市松北区税务局副局长；蔡秀瑛是黑河市市委宣传部干部。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，朱鸣镝与蔡秀瑛被大庆市公安局国保跨地区抓捕。在关押期间，朱鸣镝与蔡秀瑛夫妻二人被秘密带到哈尔滨松北区某宾馆，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月中旬，朱鸣镝和蔡秀瑛被“取保候审”回家。因朱鸣镝和蔡秀瑛的很多个人物品，包括私家车，被大庆龙南分局抢走。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月初，朱鸣镝与龙南分局栾姓局长联系，要求退还个人财物。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，朱鸣镝接到电话，让他们夫妇二人带着身份证去龙南分局取被扣押的东西。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，朱鸣镝和蔡秀瑛去了大庆龙南分局，结果他们被欺骗，再次被抓捕。此后，朱鸣镝和蔡秀瑛夫妇被批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月末，朱鸣镝和蔡秀瑛夫妇在大庆法院被视频开庭，被分别判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月和<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，分别被罚金<span lang="EN-US">6</span>万和<span lang="EN-US">7</span>万。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2032</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/3/3/457349.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/3/3/457349.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">蔡玉嫦：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">广东省汕头市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1952</span>年生，家住汕头市龙湖区外砂镇莲中村。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月二十日，中共开始疯狂迫害法轮功后，原本幸福温馨的家，被中共迫害得支离破碎。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日被警察抓捕；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日被金平区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金一万元；蔡玉嫦提起上诉；汕头市中级法院<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日枉法维持原判。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日左右，蔡玉嫦被关押到广东省女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/10/11/450658.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/10/11/450658.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">蔡予华</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：河南省三门峡市法轮功学员，女，二零二一年四月左右被判刑四年半，现已被劫持到河南省新乡女子监狱。蔡予华由于坚定修炼法轮功，在<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年前被中共劳教（具体时间不详）。蔡予华由于在<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月向最高法院和检察院邮寄控告迫害元凶江泽民的控告信，同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日晚上被抓捕、关押，家人被勒索财物，后又被判刑，在新乡女子监狱，受尽折磨，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年出狱。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，蔡予华向有关部门邮寄了申诉控告信，要求返还并按时发放她在判刑期间被剥夺的养老保险金。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月初，蔡予华被三门峡陕州区警察从家中抓捕，关押在三门峡市看守所，至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年半，后被送往新乡女子监狱继续关押迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">蔡玉英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1955</span>年生，长春市农安县法轮功学员，农民。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日清晨六点多钟，在农安县政府大楼对面，一群国保公安人员抓捕一家三口——蔡玉英、于娇茹母女，和这家老实巴交的男主人。那天，农安县非法抓捕了二十多名法轮功学员。此次非法抓捕行动，是由长春市政法委和农安县政法委共同策划实施的，长春市政法委书记马延峰亲赴农安县部署非法抓捕行动，七月十三日，农安县政法委、“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”召开会议落实具体行动方案。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日判决书下到看守所：蔡玉英被判<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/27/2021-9-27.html<o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; tab-stops: 122.5pt; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">蔡智慧</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">黑龙江省哈尔滨市双城区法轮功学员，</span>蔡智慧在<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被吉林警察抓捕到吉林省的看守所，后获悉其被吉林法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<u><span lang="EN-US">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/13/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%81%E4%BA%8C%E6%9C%88%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%89%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-434767.html</span></u><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">曹爱兰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1953</span>年生，河南南阳油田法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年她修炼法轮大法。一九九九年七月二十日，中共开始疯狂迫害法轮功，曹爱兰因为坚持信仰法轮大法，曾四次被绑架，两次判刑，累计陷冤狱<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>至<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，河南省南阳市公安局采取统一行动，在南阳地区开始绑架法轮功学员，两陷冤狱的法轮功学员曹爱兰老太被抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，曹爱兰被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，罚金三万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">曹长起：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">山东省临沂市蒙阴县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年已年过七旬。其于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日被抓捕、关押，后得知他被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，已经被劫持到山东男子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/6/16/444998.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/6/16/444998.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">曹春生：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1979</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日出生，河南省郑州市高新区石佛办事处百炉屯村大街<span lang="EN-US">159</span>号居民，私营塑料制品生产经营业主，抗暴维权者、中国在押维权人士。自<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月以来，其房屋一直被郑州市高新区石佛办事处政府威胁强拆，部分财产已遭损坏，出于无奈，自此其走上拆迁维权之路；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，其住房在被镇政府暴力强拆时家人竟被打伤；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，其所开办工厂再次遭当地政府强拆；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，一批手持各种器械及大型机械的强拆者欲将其剩余房屋进行野蛮强拆，为保护家园，其全家奋起反抗，双方随发生激烈冲突，混乱中为了自卫，其将对方其中二人刺伤，最终导致一死一伤，自己也在冲突中受伤，之后逃走；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，其被郑州警方在三门峡市灵宝县以涉嫌“故意伤害罪”拘捕，并关押于郑州市第三看守所；另有一名远房亲戚也因其在逃亡中曾在他家待过而被警方以涉嫌“窝藏罪”刑拘；据悉，其与强拆方发生冲突时，有村民远距离拍下一些照片和证据，后来不幸均被警方没收销毁；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，其案被郑州市中牟县检察院起诉至郑州市中牟县法院；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，终被郑州市中牟县法院以“故意伤害罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。目前在河南省焦南监狱（河南焦作市映湖路焦南监狱，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">454003</span>）服刑。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/8.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/8.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">曹干：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">大名曹福果，湖北黄石市法轮功学员，男，一九九五年开始修炼法轮功。一九九九年七月中共疯狂地在全国发动对法轮功的迫害，曹干和妻子王月梅先后两次被关押到劳教所、洗脑转化班迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月的曹干退休金全部被停发。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，警察闯入曹干家中将曹干抓捕到黄石市第一看守所。<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月中旬开庭，曹干被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月。<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月份曹干被关押到湖北荆门沙洋范家台监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/01/110.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/01/110.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">曹进兴：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1951</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年生，唐山市农机局退休职工。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，在中共当局的“敲门行动”中，他被唐山市路北区文化路派出所警察绑架。警察非法抄家持续了三个小时，家中大量私人物品被抢劫。在警察绑架过程中，曹进兴被摔伤，缝了几针。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，被批捕，在唐山市第一看守所被关押一年多，后背生了很多皮疹。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，河北唐山市路北区一审判处曹进兴有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 271.0pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">曹培植：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1960</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年代出生，河南省义马市人，六四亲历者，《零八宪章》第<span lang="EN-US">10</span>批签署人，原“温馨小屋”群主，社会时政关注者，民主异见人士，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">1989</span>年，曾因参与年天安门民主运动并亲历“六四惨案”，遂自此改变了人生轨迹，坚定的走上一条中国民主运动不归路；曾因以民主推手、民权精英、博客骑士自许，而创建“温馨小屋”博客群，并在其努力经营下，使该博客群的点击量高达<span lang="EN-US">70</span>万人次；也正是因其频发民主信息和对中共当局不利的时政批评性信息，故而引起河南省当局的极度不悦与伺机打击；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，因其在微信群里传播“未经官方证实的海外消息，并对党和国家领导人有侮辱性言论”，遂被河南省义马市警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留；同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，又被义马市检察院以同罪名正式批捕；被押至今，一直无律师介入，家属急盼介入。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">曹培植于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日被法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。曹培植此次被抓的起因是在他建的微信群“温馨小屋”评论习近平及他的执政方针。法院说判决书和起诉书不让家属带走，只让家人看一眼。家属还没有看到起诉书和判决书。<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">目前被羁押于河南省渑池县看守所（河南省三门峡市渑池县英豪镇英东村，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">472434</span>）。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 271.0pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/12/blog-post_27.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/12/blog-post_27.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 271.0pt;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/07/26.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/07/26.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">曹萍<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span><span lang="EN-US"> </span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">西安康市法轮功学员<span lang="EN-US">,</span>女。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日法轮功学员曹萍、陈军、杜凤英外出时被安康市岚皋县公安警察抓捕、构陷，后遭刑事拘留、批捕、起诉，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日被开庭<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，曹萍被旬阳法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万，没收抄家所得的全部私人财产（其中还有四万元用于养老金）。曹萍女士目前被关押在汉滨区看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2030</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/11/8.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/11/8.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 271.0pt;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/11/4/%E9%99%95%E8%A5%BF%E5%AE%89%E5%BA%B7%E5%B8%82%E6%9B%B9%E8%90%8D%E7%AD%89%E4%B8%89%E4%BD%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%BA%94%E8%87%B3%E5%85%AB%E5%B9%B4-467856.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/11/4/%E9%99%95%E8%A5%BF%E5%AE%89%E5%BA%B7%E5%B8%82%E6%9B%B9%E8%90%8D%E7%AD%89%E4%B8%89%E4%BD%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%BA%94%E8%87%B3%E5%85%AB%E5%B9%B4-467856.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">曹三强</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：祖籍湖南，曾在当地创立家庭教会，是“中国福音会”牧师。<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年汶川地震后，曾从事四川基督教爱心工作，帮助学生及地震灾民度过难关。多年前，曹三强到云南普洱从事宣教、慈善救济及兴教办学事业，并在当地创办多所学校，帮助贫困儿童入学。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，他与基督徒景如霞从缅甸佤邦（缅甸第二特区）返国时，出于便利使用了非正式方式入境中国，被边防武警拦截拘捕，<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日即被当地检察院以涉嫌“偷越国境罪”批捕。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日该案移送检察院审查起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日该案在孟连县法院开庭，曹三强的亲友参加了旁听。尽管曹三强的辩护人刘培福律师认为，其当事人的行为不应构成犯罪，但他仍于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日被云南省孟连县法院以“偷越国境罪”重判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元人民币，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。另一位基督徒景如霞被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，处罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元，已当庭释放。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月获刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年的曹三强牧师已转到位于云南省昆明市东郊王大桥的昆明监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/05/5.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/05/5.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">曹生祥：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">青海西宁市法轮功学员。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">2022</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">年六十六岁，本是西宁交通医院后勤科科长。因修炼法轮功，曾遭判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日被西宁城北区公安抓捕，再次被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，目前被关押在门源监狱（海北州浩门监狱）。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="http://4.31.18.88/mh/articles/2022/3/22/%E9%9D%92%E6%B5%B7%E8%A5%BF%E5%AE%81%E5%B8%82%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E6%9B%B9%E7%94%9F%E7%A5%A5%E5%86%8D%E9%81%AD%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E5%85%A5%E7%8B%B1-440336.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">http://4.31.18.88/mh/articles/2022/3/22/%E9%9D%92%E6%B5%B7%E8%A5%BF%E5%AE%81%E5%B8%82%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E6%9B%B9%E7%94%9F%E7%A5%A5%E5%86%8D%E9%81%AD%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E5%85%A5%E7%8B%B1-440336.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">曹艳芬：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，五十多岁，吉林省榆树市法轮功学员。曹艳芬<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日被吉林市船营区公安分局欢喜岭派出所警察抓捕，关押在吉林市看守所，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年后，已被劫入吉林省女子监狱继续迫害。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">曹永亮：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1981</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日出生，县人，山西省汾西县永安镇郭村村民，职业不详，维权人士，中国在押维权人士。曾因汾西县政府在炸无证黑煤窑时，将住宅房屋震塌，且无人赔偿，自此走上维权上访之路，期间曾多次遭遇拘留，其户口本亦因累次上访而被警方恶意没收；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，曾因在京上访时遭截访、欺骗和毒打等迫害，地方当局先是答应给其赔偿<span lang="EN-US">6</span>万元，并当场支付现金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元，打欠条<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元，但将其带到北京市长安西街派出所后，即遭警方毒和搜身，致其后来长期身体虚弱、吐血不止、大小便流血，其刚拿到的<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元赔偿金亦被抢走、<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元欠条被撕毁，随后被汾西县警方拘留<span lang="EN-US">20</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，曾因继续上访又被右安门派出所警方毒打，并被汾西县警方拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；此后，再次因上访而被拘留<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次，且每次都是<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，当其在北京打工之时，被前来的汾西县警方突然抓回老家，遭毒打后被关至临汾市尧都区吴村看守所；同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，即被汾西县警方以“伪造居民身份证、寻衅滋事罪”刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，被汾西县检察院正式批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被山西省汾西县法院以“伪造身份证罪、寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；据悉，看守所关押期间，屡受非人折磨，曾被毒打导致其头破血流，眼睛看不见，眉骨骨折；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，刑满获释；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，山西省汾西县当局因惧怕其在“百年党庆”时期再到北京上访，影响党国形象，随指派当地警方为其提供生活困难补助<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元，以令其立刻中止去京上访；同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，因其认为中共“百年党庆”敏感期已过，遂就到国家信访局继续提交申诉材料，岂料<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日在北京暂住地遭遇截访；遣回原籍之后，先是送山西省蒲县看守所被拒收，又于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日被送乡宁县隔离，自此失联；<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个多月后，在其家人委托的律师努力打听下终于获知，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日<span lang="EN-US">-21</span>日，其案被山西省汾西县法院庭审宣判，最终被以“敲诈勒索罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。目前被羁押于山西省临汾市尧都区看守所<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">。信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/5_22.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/5_22.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">曹中荣：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">湖北大冶市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日晚上，曹中荣被恶警撬门抓捕，被关押在大冶看守所长达十个多月。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年底被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，过年后将被关押到监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<b>信息来</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/2/14/456770.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/2/14/456770.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">操科：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">西安基督徒，受洗已<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年。他因遵循圣教导，积极参与各类社会救助，支援过新乡山西水灾、上海疫情，帮助过孤儿难民，也参与教会的福音事工。因为传播福音工作，他于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日中午<span lang="EN-US">12:30 </span>左右，被湖南郴州市警方以非法经营的罪名带走并刑事拘。操科的代理律师三次赴郴州市看守所依法要求会见，看守所均已其在提审中，予以拒绝。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/08/blog-post_79.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/08/blog-post_79.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">常昊：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">云南省昭通市镇雄县基督教传道。常昊在<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>号下午<span lang="EN-US">6</span>点过被昭通镇雄的公安带走，先说是行政拘留，后说是刑事拘留。家属没有收到任何拘留通知书。罪名是寻衅滋事罪。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/04/blog-post_69.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/04/blog-post_69.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">常珈瑄：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1970</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，山西省临汾市人，退役军人，临汾市尧都区解放西路<span lang="EN-US">54</span>号“常家大院”（祖宅）继承人之一，著名维权公民，维权致残者，人权捍卫者，中国在押维权人士。自<span lang="EN-US">1953</span>年以来，因其从清代传承下来的祖宅曾被山西省晋南专区地方国营建筑工程队借走，历经数十载后，借方竟不想再谈归还之事，其父常耀文遂被迫携其全家人走上投诉维权之路<span lang="EN-US">1992</span>年，其父带着妻儿数十人举家欲迁回祖宅居住，租房方不仅不如约归还，反以昔日领导“现在都管不了”为由久拖不给，其父无奈，同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，随一纸诉状将临汾市建筑工程总公司告上地方法院；同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，临汾市人民法院派人向当年的证人、中保等数人取证，经过比对，认为证词皆与常耀文所诉情况一致，所以于<span lang="EN-US">1993</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，法院对其案双方进行了调解；不料被告方一边应诉，一边却仍与中国建行银行临汾市支行办理房屋交割手续，临汾市法院针此最终判定：“买卖无效，撤销其违法买卖涉及本案房产的有关手续”；被告方（又即借房方）不服，提起上诉，后经临汾市中级法院二审裁决：支持一审裁判；但借房方仍不服判决，反复几次提起上诉，而当地的政府土地部门亦对此事久拖<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年不予裁定 ；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年，因临汾市建筑工程总公司谎称“上世纪<span lang="EN-US">50</span>年代已购得<span lang="EN-US">54</span>号院，<span lang="EN-US">1992</span>年被常耀文占用并在此院内违法建筑，<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年临汾市国土资源局确权该院国有土地使用权归属该公司”，并以此为由将其父枉法诬告上法庭，要求其父“停止侵权、恢复原状、返还财产”；此案件被受理后，尧都区法院一审以“原告起诉状中涉及的违法建筑应当由有关行政执法部门查处，不属于法院民事受案范围”，驳回了该借房公司的起诉；该公司仍然不服，再次上诉，又经临汾市中级法院终审裁定：一审的裁定驳回起诉正确；但遗憾的是，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，其父常耀文未等来土地证即与世长辞。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，其母再度委托律师、其及其姊常春枝，提出土地权属申请；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，临汾市国土资源局受理了该案件，但此后除<span lang="EN-US">2</span>次发出延期调查处理通知书之外，一直未予办结；其全家在维权诉讼过程中，曾屡遭殴打侮辱，导致其父受伤卧床不起，其被临汾市规划局打断四根肋骨，成了残疾人；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，其姐弟二人相继被临汾市警方抓捕，并被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”、“妨碍公务罪”指定居所监视居住；后被正式逮捕被羁押于临汾市尧都区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月获悉，常珈瑄因抗强拆，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，现在山西晋城监狱二监区服刑。何时开庭何时宣判，一概不知。同时被捕的其姐常春枝怎样，目前情况不详。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/10/5.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/10/5.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">常玮平：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1984</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日出生，陕西省宝鸡市凤翔县城关镇周家门前村人，原陕西立刚律师事务所执业律师，人权律师，人权捍卫者，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">早年曾就读于重庆大学；毕业后，<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年—<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年，通过一系列的律师资格自修和考试，最终获取律师执业资格证，后在陕西立刚律师事务所成为正式律师；工作期间，不仅曾代理多起公益诉讼（含艾滋歧视、乙肝歧视、性别歧视等）案件，亦曾代理过多起诸如“无锡<span lang="EN-US">4</span>·<span lang="EN-US">13</span>寻衅滋事案”、“无锡访民王金娣寻衅滋事案”、“南京王健寻衅滋事案”等敏感人权及弱势群体维权案件；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，曾因此而被陕西宝鸡司法局停业<span lang="EN-US"> 3 </span>个月；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22 </span>日，其律师资格证被当地律师事务所注销；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年，在停业期满后，其基本处于无法在其他律师事务所获得工作机会的状态，因其曾在陕西省境内与至少<span lang="EN-US">10</span>家律师事务所接洽，但皆不顺利，或即将签约时临时变卦，或虽签约后又突然解除合约；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，曾因参加了一个与多名维权律师和异见人士在厦门的非正式私人聚会，后因被中共官方知晓后定性为“厦门聚会案”，多人遭严打狠抓，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，其亦被陕西省宝鸡市警方跨省抓走，并被以“危害国家安全”为由指定居所监视居住；后被取保候审，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，又因对外发视频称其在拘押期间，遭受酷刑，即每天（<span lang="EN-US">24</span>小时<span lang="EN-US">/</span>次）都把他绑在一种叫做“老虎凳”的刑具上，连续审问<span lang="EN-US">16</span>次，致其右手拇指到食指至今都毫无知觉，且在取保获释后仍受到严密监视等，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，随再次被陕西省宝鸡市警方抓走，后被以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”指定居所监视居住；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，被宝鸡市检察院以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”予以批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，其案在陕西省宝鸡市凤县法院秘密开庭，其妻子前往要求参加旁听，遭警方恶意围堵；<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，终被宝鸡市凤县法院一审以“颠覆国家政权罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月。此前被羁押于宝鸡市凤县看守所。现在已经转监到陕西省渭南监狱。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/09/36.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/09/36.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">常卫云：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河南新乡维权人士，女，汉族，<span lang="EN-US">1962</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日出生，河南省封丘县曹岗乡清河集村人。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，深夜聚众入室行凶的“反杀案”案发——那是因为常卫云家举报乡镇贪腐问题，遭到非法入室殴打。那夜为防卫自身安全对非法入室者进行还击，丈夫儿子正当防卫杀了人，随后丈夫儿子双双入狱。常卫云为丈夫儿子奔走十多年呼吁喊冤。此前，常卫云在微博上举报新乡市乡镇官员千万别墅，存在腐败现象，无人问津，她维权上访十几年却遭到打击报复，长期在北京流浪住在桥洞下，为维持生计到处奔波劳碌，奔波在各大信访窗口，问题没有得到解决。随后，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日常卫云因在微博快手上举报贪官遭到抓捕，目前常卫云遭到打击报复已经由行政拘留转刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/08/blog-post_82.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/08/blog-post_82.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">常秀娥：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">宁夏中卫市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1969</span>年出生，个体工商户，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日因控告江泽民，被中卫市公安局沙坡头分局行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">8</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日因向他人讲法轮功、做三退，被中卫市公安局沙坡头分局行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">13</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日被中卫市公安局沙坡头分局警察抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被沙坡头区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">7</span>千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/5/20/461058.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/5/20/461058.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">常玉春：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">男、<span lang="EN-US">1968</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日出生，曾用名常玉光，陕西省西安市人，西安市高陵区泾渭上城小区<span lang="EN-US">41</span>号楼<span lang="EN-US">1</span>单元<span lang="EN-US">3</span>层<span lang="EN-US">10</span>号公民，基督徒，陕西光义爱圣印务公司法人代表，中国在押良心犯。自<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月起，因其所属印务公司大量印刷了与基督教信仰有关的数据及图书，随引起地方当局的高度关注与警惕；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，西安市文化执法部门联合西安市国家安全部门对其公司进行了查封与鉴定，现场扣押各种宗教类书籍<span lang="EN-US">21</span>万余册，后又经陕西省新闻出版和电影质量检测中心对其中《改革宗信仰》等<span lang="EN-US">24</span>种图书鉴定，认定该<span lang="EN-US">24</span>种图书为“未经批准擅自印刷的出版物”的非法出版物，随于次日（<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日），立刻与其妻李琛慧被西安市高陵区警方一并抓走，后被以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”指定居所监视居住；同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，又被更换罪名以涉嫌“非法经营罪”刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，被西安市高陵区检察院以同罪名予以批捕，指控其在无印刷许可证的情况下经营印刷业务，印刷非法出版物，扰乱市场秩序，起行为均构成非法经营罪，故而应予以逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，被西安市高陵区法院一审以“非法经营罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">25</span>万元；其不服上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，经陕西省西安市中级法院二审裁决，最终仍然驳回上诉，维持原判，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。目前仍被羁押于西安市高陵区看守所，未来将在何监狱服刑，暂不明晰。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">苏州市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1972</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日出生，家住苏州市浒墅关镇。<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>年修炼法轮大法修炼。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月中共迫害法轮功后，常铮和母亲常桂凤多次遭抓捕、抄家，当地警察和居委会人员无数次上门骚扰她们。常铮<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月被抓捕，后被判刑。因常铮单身，当地没有直系亲属，她遭迫害的情况外界一无所知，更无法给她送钱、送衣物。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/5/19/461025.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年开始就清水电站移民的补偿安置权益，不服地方法院的枉法裁判而进京上访，遭到地方政府、公安派出所无数次的截访，及非法拘禁黑监狱。后来，认识了竹山县双台乡鱼塘村的陈柏清，就委托陈柏清代理撰写举报控告材料。因其在潘口水电站移民时的安置补偿权益遭到损害而上访，在<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年年的<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月初到省会武汉市举报控告镇、村官吏的违法行为，被押回当地竹山县上庸镇福利院黑监狱。陈柏清<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月被以“涉嫌寻衅滋事罪”拘留、抄家。<b>信息来源：<span
