mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈翠珠：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广东省湛江市雷州市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1962</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月生。<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>年开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日晚，陈翠珠因参加集体学法时被湛江市赤坎区警察入屋抓捕，恶警在她家中搜到资料及其辛苦工作积攒下来的现金及存折，声称这是法轮功的经费，企图以此关押构陷。后将她关押在湛江市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日其被警察用手铐脚镣连铐、头脚几乎碰在一起的所谓“庭审”，<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月被湛江市赤坎区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，并罚款<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;"> </span></b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/7/1/462528.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/7/1/462528.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><a name="_Hlk54957732"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈迪才：</span></b></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk54957732;"></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1982</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年生，大学文化，户籍所在地是黄石市下辖阳新县黄颡口镇。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日晚，他的姐姐被她丈夫李生水家暴殴打，外甥女打电话给舅舅陈迪才打电话，随后陈迪才骑车到姐家，看见姐姐被打得躺在床上，地上有被扯下的几缕头发。陈迪才与姐夫李生水理论，李生水打电话举报陈迪才炼法轮功。晚十一点左右，黄石市黄石港区红旗桥派出所警察把陈迪才和她姐一家带到派出所，在陈迪才身上搜出几张真相币和含有法轮功内容的<span lang="EN-US">U</span>盘，派出所立即联系了黄石港区国保大队。陈迪才被关押、构陷一年多，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被视频开庭，以捏造的「事实」判处陈迪才<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年有期徒刑，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: PMingLiU; mso-fareast-language: ZH-TW; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈法庆</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">浙江环保人士。<span lang="EN-US">50</span>岁，农民企业家出身。<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年前，他曾经和江苏省环保人士吴立红自费在“纽约时报”刊登中英文环保公益广告，敦促当时刚上任的政治局常委，兑现环保承诺。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，陈法庆被当局以“组织领导传销活动”为由，刑事拘留。家属认为，该事件与中共十九大即将召开有关。家属称，陈法庆多年来不断受到当局打压，谋生遇到很多障碍。不到<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月前，他曾向习近平寄送锦旗，要求他及各级领导善待残疾人。后案件讯息全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈公安：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">江西省九江市人，九江市武宁县人，民主维权公民，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">因与所当地多名民主维权公民经常聚集聊天议事，并积极在微信群里发时政性贴文及视频讯息，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，遂与王林安、李玉荣和柯有斌等另<span lang="EN-US">3</span>名民主维权好友分别被九江地区国保警方传唤带走，次日均被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留，自此失联；同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，其案被九江市武宁县警方提交到当地武宁县检察院，被检察院以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”正式批捕；截至当前，其被抓之后的各种具体信息均称不详，亦不知有否律师介入；与其熟识的网友指称，其被逮捕，应与中共二十大召开之际其等网络言论令当局不安有关，故而因言获罪。今获悉其获刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。目前被羁押于九江市武宁县看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/06/16.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/06/16.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; text-decoration: none; text-underline: none;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈桂莲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广西钦州市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1957</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>年开始修炼法轮功，广西钦州市钦南区人，以前住在防城港，后来居住钦南区东南社区。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月被钦南区南珠派出所抓捕、关押构陷。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年、罚金两万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/5/20/%E5%B9%BF%E8%A5%BF%E9%92%A6%E5%B7%9E%E5%B8%82%E9%99%88%E6%A1%82%E8%8E%B2%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4-461047.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/5/20/%E5%B9%BF%E8%A5%BF%E9%92%A6%E5%B7%9E%E5%B8%82%E9%99%88%E6%A1%82%E8%8E%B2%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4-461047.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈海霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">广东法轮功学员。广东雷州市白沙镇梛楠村人，后在湛江霞山区租住，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月末，在雷州市向民众发放法轮功资料的时候，被告，遭关押了几天后，获释，回到自己租住的房子。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月初，陈海霞又被警察绑架、抄家。后遭判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。在血压高不适合关押的情况下，中院维持冤判，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被关押到广州女子监狱迫害。目前，陈海霞被洗脑灌输、野蛮灌食，眼睛赤红、非常憔悴，仅一个月余，其境况令家人十分担忧。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈皓恒：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1996</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，中华人民共和国（香港）籍人，“雨伞运动”参与者，香港政党“社会民主连线”（简称“社民连线”或“社民连”）成员，前立法会议员助理，原“民间人权阵线（民阵）”召集人，民主派政治人士，中国在押政治犯。自小生长于香港，并从初中开始，因接触、了解到“六四”的历史而对社会政治产生浓厚兴趣，曾先加入中学生组织多次参与政治活动；中学毕业后，虽一度攻读旅游专业，但自从<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年参与“雨伞运动”之后决定辍学全程投入社会运动，故而自此加入香港民主政党“社民连”，并参与其他民主派组织，曾做过立法会议员助理，协助其参与竞选工作；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年，曾因前民阵召集人岑子杰被香港国安局警方关押，迫于形势需要新人补位，其随接手民阵召集人一职；又因该组织原是结合香港众多民主派政党及公民团体的平台，但自其担任召集人之后，有消息盛传民阵可能卷入一场《国安法》案件，随民主党、公民党等香港主流政党被迫先后宣布退出，致使民阵变得更为孤军作战；后又因其多次参与“反送中”游行示威，让其累积不少筹办大型活动的经验，包括如何向警方申请游行、怎样联络媒体、怎样摆放街站、撰写和发布声明等等，故而数月以来，民阵的中坚力量虽只剩下其一个人，但依然把工作做到很好；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年，因“港区国安法”的出台和实施促使香港爆发了大规模的“反送中”示威抗议活动，反对北京缩减香港自由的示威民众情绪激昂；同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，因其深度参加了民主派港人的国庆节大游行和反送中抗议行动，被港警拘捕，被控涉嫌涉嫌“组织未经批准集结罪”和“煽惑他人参与未经批准集结罪”等共计<span lang="EN-US">14</span>项罪名；后经几次香港区域法院提堂庭审，先被获刑<span lang="EN-US">18</span>个月，且已入监服刑；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，又被香港东区法院再行审判，被指控因参与<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年在港岛区的非法集结，被判刑期<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，鉴于其承认该控罪，最终法官判处其在原有刑期上加刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个月，共被判囚<span lang="EN-US">22</span>个月。目前疑似在香港赤柱监狱服刑。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/05/22.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/05/22.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">陈恒：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">福州法轮功学员。于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日被连江县城关派出所警察抓捕，被转到罗源县隔离十几天后，再被转关到连江县看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，他被逮捕。长乐检察院<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日将他起诉到长乐法院。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，陈恒收到长乐法院对他判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年的判决书。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/10/9/450587.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/10/9/450587.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈洪伟：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1968</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日出生，别名陈宏伟，辽宁省康平县人，康平县体校家属楼北栋<span lang="EN-US">5</span>单元<span lang="EN-US">501</span>号公民，辽宁伟业律师事务所律师，贪腐举报人，维权律师，中国在押维权人士。自成为执业律师并在辽宁伟业律师事务所任职以来，一直勤勉工作，认真执业；<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年，曾因康平县开发区管委会与开发区朝阳工业园内养殖小区的被拆迁户谈判陷入僵局，被该管委会聘请为法务工作代理，前去与被拆迁户协商拆迁事宜；为支持政府工作，其接受了此一聘请委托，并以先难后易等方式耐心做到与拆迁户的协商工作；<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月—<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，曾先后三次从开发区财政局借款共计<span lang="EN-US">103</span>万元，且自搭<span lang="EN-US">1.46</span>万元，全部如数如约支付给被拆迁户作为补偿款，得到众被拆迁户的广泛认可；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，曾因对当地政府的招标行为及相关部门官员的贪腐问题不满，声称要对县里的主要领导温某予以举报，随后不久立遭打击报复；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，被沈阳市辽中区警方以涉嫌“行贿罪”抓捕，后被留置；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，又被以涉嫌“贪污罪、行贿罪”转为刑拘，后知被疑指与十几年前其协助当地开发区拆迁和送某领导洗浴卡有关；同年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，被沈阳市和平区检察院以同罪名予以批捕，并被关押于沈阳市和平区看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，被沈阳市辽中区法院一审以“贪污罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并处罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">20</span>万元；以“行贿罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，并处罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">10</span>万元；以“诈骗罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年，并处罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">50</span>万元，数罪并罚决定执行有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年，并处罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">80</span>万元；其不服判决，立即上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，经沈阳市中级法院二审裁决，驳回上诉，维持原判；其坚称无罪，再次提起申诉；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，经沈阳市中级法院再审，依然维持原判，驳回申诉；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2033</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。目前仍被羁押于沈阳市和平区看守所，未来将在何监狱服刑尚不明晰。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-style: italic; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">陈鸿元</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-style: italic; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：男，广东揭阳法轮功学员。家住揭阳市榕城区东兴街道。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，他被榕城区国保、榕东派出所警察抓捕，关押到揭阳市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日他被非法批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年底，他被揭东区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，罚金八万元。陈鸿元不服，提出上诉。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，揭阳市中级法院维持原判。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，陈鸿元被关押到广东省四会监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/7/2022-3-7.html#zip2"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/7/2022-3-7.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">陈华良：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">男广东省惠州市博罗县法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1957</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月出生，贵州省贵阳市人，家住贵阳市云岩区狮子路。他<span lang="EN-US">1980</span>年毕业于浙江省金华供销学校并留校任教，<span lang="EN-US">1991</span>年调任贵州商学院任教师。因坚持修炼法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，他被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，被开除公职。陈华良在灵泉学堂教国学。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日上午<span lang="EN-US">11</span>时左右，博罗县公安局国保大队几乎倾巢出动，和九潭派出所警察一块，以查经营为由，从邻居家闯入灵泉学堂，查抄。查抄中，发现有法轮功书籍，警察将赵天华抓捕，他的妻子蔡惠斌、灵泉学堂的教师陈华良、练日光一起被抓捕，被关押到博罗县看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被惠州市惠城区法院判决：陈华良被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/11/9/451690.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/11/9/451690.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈继海：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吉林市法轮功学员。男，<span lang="EN-US">1954</span>年生，家住吉林市丰满区二道乡张家村。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，吉林市公安局及下属派出所警察抓捕至少有<span lang="EN-US">21</span>名法轮功学员、二名家属，法轮功学员陈继海、宋德满是其中两位。被关押一年余，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，陈继海和宋德满分别被判<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年和<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，现在吉林省第二监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈家鸿：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1966</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月出生，广西壮族自治区北流县隆盛镇平坡村人，又名陈文胆，字数真，早年为广西北流县鸭壤小学教师，知名业余书法家、字画家，原南宁市百举鸣律师事务所执业律师，敏感案件代理人，中国人权律师团成员，人权律师，政治犯。自从成为“百举鸣律师事务所”（现已被当局取缔）中一名执业律师以来，因长期参与维权敏感案件，追求民主人权并为之积极发声，随屡遭中共当局严打逼迫；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，曾因积极介入了震惊网络的“广西村民罗继标在看守所离奇死亡事件”，而遭广西警方的持枪围困；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，曾因同一事件，其介入维权行为被广西律师协会视为违规，从而被该律师协会给予“公开谴责行业处分的通报”；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，又被南宁市司法局行政处罚停业半年；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，其被北流县警方以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”抓捕、刑拘，其家被查抄；之后，其又被北流县检察院以同罪由予以批捕，并被指控因其反对官员腐败、呼吁建立民主宪政等带有政治倾向的公开言论、书法作品及行为艺术等涉及挑战现政权，尤其是其中一副书法作品，内含“成立暗杀突击队！清算邪恶官僚，加速民主进程”等激进敏感字眼，触犯了政府的相关法律条例，其行为属于违法；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，其案件被地方检察院移交至玉林巿中级法院起诉；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，终被玉林市中级法院在其辩护律师未到场的情况下，一审以“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日；此前被羁押于广西玉林市看守所。陈家鸿<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，被传唤，后又被刑事拘留，涉嫌罪名“寻衅滋事”，办案机关是广西北流市治安大队。家人噤声，目前尚无律师介入。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/10/34.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/10/34.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈剑雄：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">原名陈进新，<span lang="EN-US">1974</span>年出生，湖北省赤壁市人，网名陈剑雄，“赤壁五君子”之一，南方街头运动践行者，民主维权公民，中国在押政治犯。自<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年以来，曾多次参与国内的围观声援活动，勇于多次举牌、拉横幅表达对民主宪政的政治要求，是南方街头运动杰出代表之一，亦因此曾多次遭到中共警方的拘留、刑拘、酷刑和强行驱赶等；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，曾因与袁小华、袁奉初、黄文勋等民主维权者在湖北省赤壁市宣传民主政治，而被当地警方以“煽动颠覆国家政权”为由刑拘，<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日被取保获释；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，曾与民主维权者谢文飞在广东省佛山市街头举横幅，要求“废除一党专制，建立民主中国”，而被佛山警方再次以“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”刑拘，并关押在天河区看守所，备受酷刑折磨，<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被取保获释；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月，曾因参加山东曲阜薛福顺非正常死亡事件观察团奔赴曲阜追查真相，多次在曲阜遭警方欧打和驱赶；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，曾因到黑龙江省声援“建三江律师被拘事件”，而被当警方行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，曾因到武汉市与多名友人会见佛教法师徐志强，被武汉警方抓走，又被以“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”刑拘，<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被取保候审；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，因再次前往河南郑州参与公民声援“郑州十君子事件”，并到河南焦作市声援“张小玉夫妇杀警事件”，遂于<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被警方在郑州第三看守所附近抓走，且被湖北省赤壁市警方直接报检察院以涉嫌“扰乱社会公共秩序罪”执行逮捕，羁押于赤壁市看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，被湖北省咸宁市赤壁市法院以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，刑满释放；出狱后，其追求民主意志弥坚；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，因与维权友人袁兵、梁一鸣去赤壁市公安局国保大队投诉出狱后遭长期监控、骚扰等事宜，终因双方理念不同、争论颇激而不欢而散；<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，再次被赤壁市警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”抓捕刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，被赤壁市检察院正式批捕，并被羁押于赤壁看守所：<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，终被湖北省赤壁市法院一审以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；其不服上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，经咸宁市中级法院二审裁决，依然维持原判；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，刑满释放。此前在湖北省咸宁监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，陈剑雄又被警方抓捕。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2022</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日代理律师马纲权律师在湖北通城县检察院视频会见了被羁押的湖陈剑雄，获悉目前案件已移送湖北通城县检察院审查起诉。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/08/blog-post_45.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/08/blog-post_45.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/04/blog-post_17.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/04/blog-post_17.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈杰人：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈杰人毕业于清华大学法学院，中国资深的媒体人，先后在《南方周末》、《中国青年报》、《新京报》、《人民日报》等媒体上发表了<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>多篇评论文章。<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年以中国青年报记者身份踢爆武汉女大学生卖淫现象，造成轰动，但却被解雇；<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年作为公益时报主编，签发批评文章，触怒当局再被炒；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月因“批评政府过多”遭人民日报解除人民网江苏视窗执行总编职务。陈杰人多年来发表数千文章，希望推进新闻自由，并倡导以网络为平台的草根监督和公民表达。<span lang="EN-US"> 2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，陈杰人曾在网上公开实名举报湖南邵阳市纪委书记邓广雁严重失职和渎职。随后几天，陈杰人就下落不明，与外界失联。有消息透露，湖南公安以“涉嫌敲诈勒索、非法经营”等罪名“依法办理”陈杰人。目前，陈杰人的微信公众号显示“由用户投诉并经平台审核，涉嫌违反相关法律法规，账号已被停止使用”。后获知遭湖南警方刑事拘留。湖南省桂阳县人民法院网站发布消息：<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日下午，湖南省桂阳县人民法院公开开庭，对被告人陈杰人、陈伟人、刘敏寻衅滋事、敲诈勒索、非法经营、行贿一案宣告一审判决，对被告人陈杰人以寻衅滋事罪、敲诈勒索罪、非法经营罪、行贿罪判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年，并处罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">701</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2033</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">陈娟：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吉林省德惠市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，以有人举报为由，德惠市天台乡派出所和德惠国保联合绑架陈娟，并拘留十天，后陈娟被取保回家。迫害期间，因陈娟是做熟食生意，店铺生计需要她，家人着急营救，被德惠国保勒索五万元取保回家。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，德惠市六一零公安局国保大队将陈娟拉到德惠市民心医院检查身体，后又把她带到长春医院检查身体。当天陈娟被放回家中，并被告知称，关于她的所谓材料已递交到德惠市法院。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日被德惠市法院非法开庭，历时四十多分钟。当时没有宣判，称让陈娟回家等结果。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，吉林省长春德惠市法轮功学员陈娟被关押到长春“病监大队”。清明街与北安路交汇的长春市医院公安局设立的所谓“病监大队”，对外挂的牌子是口腔门诊，实质是迫害法轮功学员的黑窝，很多老年法轮功学员非法被关在这里遭迫害。现获悉，长春市德惠市法轮功学员陈娟已被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年半，仍被关押在“病监大队”。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/4/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E5%9B%9B%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-436399.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/4/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E5%9B%9B%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-436399.html</span></b></a></span><b mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈军：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陕西安康市法轮功学员<span lang="EN-US">,</span>男。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日法轮功学员陈军、曹萍、杜凤英外出时被安康市岚皋县公安警察抓捕、构陷，后遭刑事拘留、批捕、起诉，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日被开庭<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，陈军被旬阳法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，并处罚金三万；他从最早的岚皋县看守所转到旬阳看守所，现又被转回到岚皋县看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">:2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/11/5.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/11/5.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/11/4/%E9%99%95%E8%A5%BF%E5%AE%89%E5%BA%B7%E5%B8%82%E6%9B%B9%E8%90%8D%E7%AD%89%E4%B8%89%E4%BD%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%BA%94%E8%87%B3%E5%85%AB%E5%B9%B4-467856.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈利军：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河南省洛阳市人，基督徒，洛阳市栾川县基督教家庭教会传道人，中国在押良心犯。陈利军信仰耶稣基督，并一直致力于在教会里当传道人，传讲基督教福音；但因其所在河南省栾川县基督教家庭教会属改革宗信仰教会，一直不愿接受中共“三自”教会的管控，故而自新宗教事务条例实施以来，即成为屡遭中共当局监控逼迫的家庭教会之一；在此期间，其及教会信众均因基督教信仰问题而深受当地政府的不断骚扰、监控和打压；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，因其在网上购买了几本有关基督教信仰的书籍，遂被洛阳市栾川县警方立即带走，并以不确罪由处行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天；同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，又被以“诈骗罪”转为刑事拘留；截至当前，其一直失联，不予释放，或已被当地检察院批捕，但其妻子尚未收到其被逮捕的通知书；据悉，自从其被抓捕以来，不仅其所在教会<span lang="EN-US">100</span>多位基督徒持续遭遇打压和监控，其因是传道人并兼管教会的多重工作，故被罚款十万元。目前被羁押于河南省栾川县看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/11/blog-post_3.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/11/blog-post_3.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈丽萍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">南昌市西湖区法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1976</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，万筱萍、杨金凤在永正外街，陈丽萍在站前西路锦峰大酒店门口被东湖公安分局抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年元月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日上午，南昌市西湖区法院送达了对陈丽萍、万筱萍、杨金凤及万金莲的刑事判决书，陈丽萍、万筱萍、杨金凤<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人均被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月、罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元，万金莲被判<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元。因<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人均办理了「取保候审」，刑期均从判决执行之日起算。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">陈琳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">四川遂宁市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1974</span>年生，男，陈琳与妻子姚忠梅于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日早上被安居区国保警察、凤凰派出所等十余人抓捕，并抄家，抢劫走了<span lang="EN-US">1</span>台电脑、<span lang="EN-US">1</span>部手提电脑、两部打印机、几十本大法书籍等私人物品。陈琳、姚忠梅于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被安居区法院秘密开庭，陈琳被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元，做小生意的轿车（<span lang="EN-US">6</span>～<span lang="EN-US">7</span>万元）、电脑等私人财物被没收；姚忠梅被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚款<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元；陈琳刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/23/448001.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/23/448001.html</span></b></a></span><b><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈萍</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：重庆市沙坪坝区法轮功学员、女，<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年生，现年<span lang="EN-US">59</span>岁。自<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年在中共对法轮功持续二十多年的迫害中，陈萍因坚持修炼法轮大法，曾多次被非法关押、劳教和骚扰等迫害，关押期间曾遭残暴酷刑折磨。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日陈萍被重庆沙坪坝区公安局、国保队、<span lang="EN-US">610</span>等警察抄家、抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日被重庆市江北区法院开庭，被判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年有期徒刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/10/5_29.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/10/5_29.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/10/28/%E9%87%8D%E5%BA%86%E5%B8%82%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E9%99%88%E8%90%8D%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%BA%94%E5%B9%B4-467570.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/10/28/%E9%87%8D%E5%BA%86%E5%B8%82%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E9%99%88%E8%90%8D%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%BA%94%E5%B9%B4-467570.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈气：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，福建省福州市人，福州市鼓楼区洪山镇凤湖小区<span lang="EN-US">60</span>号公民，强拆受害者，维权访民，中国在押维权人士。早年，因自家房屋曾遭政府强拆，不安置、不赔偿，遂被迫多年赴京上访讨说法，但问题却一直得不到解决，反而成为当地各级政府的维稳对象，屡遭福州市当局围追堵截和非法拘押；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，曾因与其他访民在福州市中心的五一广场诉冤，而被鼓楼区安泰派出所警方抓走，并被关押在福州市公安局禁毒大队院内；同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，又因和多名维权民众前往美国驻华大使馆寻求救助，而曾被福建省驻京维稳人员强行遣返原籍；同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，因福州市洪山镇民众屡遭当局派出的警方、城管以及雇佣的黑社会成员实施暴力逼迁，故其等被强拆受害者自发在洪山镇凤池新村推棺材维权，以示誓死捍卫家园的决心；此举虽鼓舞了民众维权勇气，但却触及到福州市当局管理者的敏感神经，<span lang="EN-US">3</span>天之后的<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，其被福州市鼓楼区警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘，并送福州市第一看守所关押，后又被转到第二看守所续押；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，才被准予取保候审；但不久，又因此次在福建省政府、福建省高级法院门外和福州市五一广场等场所举牌维权，而于<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日被当地警方收监逮捕；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，被福州市罗源县法院以“寻衅滋事罪”枉法冤判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年；刑满出狱后，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，曾因和众多维权访民集体前去迎接维权人士严兴声出狱，放鞭炮以示庆祝，故又被福州市警方拘押；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，曾因与同是维权访民的陈芳、江心等<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人进京继续信访投诉，而在北京暂住的酒店附近突遭<span lang="EN-US">20</span>多名政府指派的黑保安围追堵截，后被野蛮截访送回原籍，且途中遭到非人道折磨和虐待；到达原籍后又被转交给另一伙恶势力团伙，任由他们将其等人非法拘禁在当地附近山沟里的一户人家，直到同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，才被扔在福州市新店镇的森林公园某山脚下；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，因中共两会期间进京上访，而被福州市当局以“寻衅滋事”为由拘禁在当地一黑监狱内，因其无法忍受看押人员对其的极端折磨和虐待，就爬到已拆除的窗户上而被路人看见，遂被报警并将现场视频发到网上，引起网民强烈关注，故而其再次被福州市鼓楼区警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘，后被福州市鼓楼区检察院以同罪名予以正式批捕和被很快起诉；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，其案在福州市鼓楼区法院开庭审理；虽当前福州市并无疫情，属低风险地区，但鼓楼区法院仍以疫情防控为由只允许其年迈老母和其女儿进入法院，观看远程视频开庭，另有其亲族成员以及多名福州维权公民前往围观和声援，但都被拦于法庭之外。目前被羁押于福州市鼓楼区看守所（又称福建省第二看守所，福建省福州市鼓楼区梅峰路<span lang="EN-US">65</span>号，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">350000</span>）。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2022</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被鼓楼法院以寻衅滋事罪判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/11/29.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/11/29.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/10/blog-post_2.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/10/blog-post_2.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈强：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河南政府信息公开申请人、知名民间维权举报打假人王清同案。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，被南阳市卧龙区警方以涉嫌“敲诈勒索罪”刑拘。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，本案被南阳市卧龙区检察院移交至南阳市卧龙区法院进行起诉；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，其王清、陈强、王聚才及韩猛<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人被以涉“敲诈勒索案”在南阳市卧龙区法院开庭受审，后陈强被该法院一审以“敲诈勒索罪”枉法重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2030</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">陈庆兰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吉林省舒兰市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1953</span>年生。家住舒兰市吉舒街道。她修炼法轮功二十多年。在中共对法轮功的疯狂迫害中，陈庆兰曾两次被劳教、丈夫孟祥富被判刑八年。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，舒兰市公安局国保警察将陈庆兰抓捕到舒兰看守所关押。丈夫孟祥富去看于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月二十四日含冤离世，终年七十岁。孟祥富离世后，警察也没让陈庆兰看丈夫最后一眼。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月初获悉：陈庆兰被中共法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年、罚金三千元。<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/11/458678.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/11/458678.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈秋菊：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川省遂宁市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1969</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日上午九点多，陈秋菊在遂宁市明霞路上给民众讲法轮功真相时，遭人恶告，被四个警察抓捕到南津路派出所，两人遭搜身、审问、照相，至下午三点多钟被放回家。陈秋菊<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月二<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日被蓬溪县法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。据悉，法官、检察官曾诱惑陈秋菊放弃法轮大法信仰，表示如签字可轻判，被她拒绝。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;"> </span></b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/7/1/462536.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/7/1/462536.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈仁林：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">江苏省常州市法轮功学员，现年（<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年）已经<span lang="EN-US">86</span>岁。退休前是铁路局工程师。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日早上，他在送《明慧周刊》时被警察抓捕，并遭抄家，常州市天宁区国保大队、当地检察院、法院互相勾结，以所谓破坏法律实施，约于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月对陈仁林老人判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">4</span>万元。随后关押到江苏省苏州监狱。如此老人结束冤刑时将届满<span lang="EN-US">93</span>岁高龄。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2030</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/6/27/462407.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/6/27/462407.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈三灵：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">安徽省界首市王集镇人，法轮功学员。因信法轮功而被多次遭界首市公安局及王集镇派出所骚扰。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月又因宣传法轮功资料而被非法拘捕，自此失联，近期得知他已被界首市检察院批捕。现被关押在安徽省阜阳市看守所。后案件音讯全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈世贵：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川成都市金牛区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日下午，杜荣、张珍华、陈世贵正在友人毛坤家做客休息，被成都市金牛区分局国保警察、茶店子派出所孟红等一伙警察疯狂砸门抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，毛坤、杜荣、张珍华、陈世贵被四川省成都市金牛区法院判刑，陈世贵判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年半，罚款<span lang="EN-US">6</span>千。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">陈树庆</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：<span lang="EN-US">1965</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日出生，浙江省富阳县人，自由撰稿人，<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年中国民主党全国筹委会负责人之一，人权活动家，<span lang="EN-US">89</span>学生。<span lang="EN-US">2014 </span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月—<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，因其多次参与民主活动，并参与联署呼吁释放包括异议人士吕耿松在内的大陆被拘捕人士，随遭到当局报复性打压，并被警方两次以“颠覆国家政权”罪由传唤；至<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，终被杭州市警方以“颠覆国家政权罪”正式刑事拘留；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，被杭州市检察院正式批捕。目前被羁押于浙江省杭州市看守所，<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日在杭州中院开庭，未判决。经延期与退侦后，此案于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日下午宣判，陈树庆被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈淑琴：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">宁夏固原市隆德县法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年生，大专文化，内科主治医师，系原隆德县医院医生。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日下午，陈淑琴给路人<span lang="EN-US">1</span>份法轮功资料让他去了解，不料被此人恶告，随后被城关派出所两个警察抓捕。隆德国保大队王胜强带人抄家及到单位搜查，抢走所有大法书籍，笔记本计算机等部份私人物品。陈淑琴当时被王胜强等人抓捕到固原市看守所，看守所拒收。国保人员给陈淑琴办了取保候审。陈淑琴回家并正常上班，大约在<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月中旬突然失踪。后获悉，陈淑琴又被抓捕、批捕。陈淑琴被关押在宁夏固原市看守所。后获悉，陈淑琴医生，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，已被关押到宁夏女子监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈书义：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河北省涞水县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1954</span>年生。河北省涞水县王村镇东王庄村人。一九九九年七月，中共发动对法轮功的残酷迫害后，老人曾两次被劳教：<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，被劳教<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，被劳教<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，时年<span lang="EN-US">66</span>岁的法轮功学员陈书义被警察入室抓捕。次日下午两点，陈书义被刑事拘留，被关押到涞水看守所至今。后获悉涿州市法院对陈书义秘密庭审，并判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。而他家人既没接到开庭通知，也没接到判决书。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">陈爽：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">23</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">岁，湖北省咸宁市人，咸宁市温泉居民，法轮功学员。因信仰和宣传法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日在深圳市龙岗区打工期间被深圳龙岗区警方非法以涉嫌邪教罪刑拘。目前被关押在深圳市龙岗区看守所。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">约于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月被深圳市龙岗区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，罚款一万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈松艳</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：女，<span lang="EN-US">1963</span>年生，黑龙江省北安市法轮功学员。她孝敬老人、家庭和睦，是遵守法律、遵守社会公德的好市民。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，陈松艳在北安市金街附近向民众讲述法轮功真相，遭不明真相的人构陷，被警察绑架。她先后被劫持到五大连池拘留所、黑河市看守所关押迫害。后遭逮捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，北安市法院在黑河市爱辉区法院对陈松艳第一次庭审。非法庭审结束时，没有宣判。后来家属被告知，陈松艳被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。陈松艳上诉到中级法院。被驳回。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈素英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">江苏南京六合区维权人士。南京市六合区横梁街道山东村杨庄<span lang="EN-US">25</span>号的农民，在<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年拖家带口到南京城谋生。同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日晚，其丈夫杨芝祥在修车铺干活时被人殴打致重伤，刚开始公安机关对杨芝祥进行鉴定后出具了轻伤的鉴定报告，不服轻伤鉴定报告的杨芝祥申请重新鉴定，结果重新鉴定居然将轻伤降级为轻微伤，杨芝祥就希望通过司法途径维权，结果各级人民法院均未公正维护其合法权益，导致失去劳动能力的杨芝祥，只能在妻子陈素英的陪伴下长驻北京申冤，而且在这条路上越陷越深。杨芝祥、陈素英夫妇俩，在<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日）到国家信访走访时，被警号为<span lang="EN-US">0204901</span>的警察带上手铐，然后通知地方截访专押回南京，后遭刑事拘留。 <span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/09/blog-post_78.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/09/blog-post_78.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈天茂：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">福建晋江维权人士。现关押在福建晋江看守所。陈案缘起于其担任合同制警察期间，在一次执行公务发生车祸而致的工伤。因工伤引发被辞退，住房被分给他人，以及待遇等纠纷，多年来陈为维权，进行了多次诉讼，多次上访，多次被拘留，又被劳教，差点被判刑。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年底前因涉嫌为境外提供国家秘密罪被逮捕，他坚定地认为自己无罪。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈卫波：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江大庆市林甸县法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1976</span>年生，女，大庆林甸县教师。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，由黑龙江省公安厅“督办”，大庆市公安局和林甸县公安局出动五十多个便衣警察，暴力抓捕了大庆市林甸县法轮功学员薛丽威、王玉红、路朝波、董娜、陈卫波等。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，大庆让胡路区法院枉法判决：路朝波、王玉红被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年、罚款七万元。薛丽威、陈卫波被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年、罚款四万元，董娜被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月、罚款三万元。关押在黑龙江省女子监狱。陈卫波刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/12/30/454021.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/12/30/454021.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">陈维权：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黑龙江鸡西市法轮功学员陈维权、潘西华夫妇，于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日遭滴道区国保金辉等警察抓捕抢劫、关押构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日被密山市法院开庭，判陈维权<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年、潘西华<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/25/%E9%BB%91%E9%BE%99%E6%B1%9F%E9%B8%A1%E8%A5%BF%E5%B8%82%E9%99%88%E7%BB%B4%E6%9D%83%E3%80%81%E6%BD%98%E8%A5%BF%E5%8D%8E%E5%A4%AB%E5%A6%87%E8%A2%AB%E8%AF%AC%E5%88%A4%E4%B8%83%E5%B9%B4%E3%80%81%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4-441692.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/25/%E9%BB%91%E9%BE%99%E6%B1%9F%E9%B8%A1%E8%A5%BF%E5%B8%82%E9%99%88%E7%BB%B4%E6%9D%83%E3%80%81%E6%BD%98%E8%A5%BF%E5%8D%8E%E5%A4%AB%E5%A6%87%E8%A2%AB%E8%AF%AC%E5%88%A4%E4%B8%83%E5%B9%B4%E3%80%81%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4-441692.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈文胜：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1969</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日出生，湖南省衡阳市石鼓区人，住衡阳市石鼓区西湖一村<span lang="EN-US">13</span>栋<span lang="EN-US">507</span>户，基督徒，湖南衡阳小群教会信徒，街头传道人，中国在押良心犯。早年曾吸毒成性十余年，后因在戒毒所听到福音而成为基督徒，并凭信心而除掉了毒瘾，故而自此致力于广传基督教福音；曾因经常举着写有“荣耀救主”、“悔改信靠得救”的十字架独自上街宣传，或与教会其他基督徒一起走街串巷，到城市闹市区（甚至到过西藏）传福音，随屡遭当局打压，多次被警方警告、威胁和被关押在衡阳市拘留所，甚至一年之中竟有<span lang="EN-US">6</span>次被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，曾因到广西壮族自治区宣传基督教福音，而被南宁市警方行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，又因上街传福音，而被湖南省衡阳市石鼓区警方行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，因与另一基督教信徒一起先后在衡阳市商业步行街附近和中医医院附近，利用喇叭、广播播放及发福音单张等方式宣传基督教，而被衡阳市蒸湘区警方以“扰乱社会秩序”为由行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，因与其母为跨农历新年传福音，而被衡阳市警方行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；之后，因其继续走街串巷传福音，而在该年又曾先后<span lang="EN-US">5</span>次被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，曾因到浙江省传福音，而被辖区警方跨境抓捕，后被指定居所监视居住于西湖山庄，<span lang="EN-US">20</span>天后，才在轮番轰炸般的约谈之后予以释放；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，因其到云南向少数民族朋友传福音，同年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，即被云南省文山壮族苗族自治州文山市警方拦截，且被移交给衡阳市警方遣回原籍；获释后，其接续外出传福音，甚至向国保警方和当地街道办事处工作人员等传福音；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，因其到湖南省益阳市安化县传福音，被衡阳市政法委、统战部及国保警方联合跨区抓回，次日被衡阳市青山派出所警方行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天；同年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，其重获自由，但释放当天又去上街传福音；据悉，其妻子、儿媳及孙女等家人因受牵连，曾遭当局多次恐吓和威胁，被要求务必说服、阻止其外出传福音，否则不仅儿媳会被单位开除公职，而且其孙女也会在将来不能考取国家公务员与教师等工作；<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，又因在街头传福音被衡阳市警方行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，期满后旋即又被以涉嫌“组织、资助非法聚集罪”刑事拘留。现羁押于衡阳市衡东县看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/09/blog-post_81.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/09/blog-post_81.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈熙涛：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江省牡丹江海林市法轮功学员。郭立彬（郭立斌）和陈熙涛夫妇，家住牡丹江市海林市蔬菜村五队，是朴实的农民，以种菜为生。因为他们坚持修炼法轮大法，在中共疯狂迫害中，郭立彬和陈熙涛多次遭中共抓捕、关押。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，海林市国保大队将郭立彬和陈熙涛抓捕、关押。后郭立彬和陈熙涛夫妇均被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，陈熙涛被劫持到黑龙江省女子监狱。郭立彬被关押在牡丹江监狱集训队迫。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/9/24/449999.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; text-decoration: none; text-underline: none;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/9/24/449999.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈晓彬：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">广东揭阳市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，广东揭阳市揭西县法轮功学员吴春雄在揭阳榕城区新河村自己的公司被揭阳市公安局东升派出所抓捕，公司的几名员工吴旭钦等也被抓捕。据悉，是公司的微信公众号出现有法轮功的真相。随后，派出所人员胁迫吴旭钦带他们到家里非法抄家，并抓捕了吴旭钦的母亲陈晓彬，还用封条把家门都封了。吴春雄原本生意很好的公司全面停运，同时很多私人物品被非法抄走。吴春雄、吴旭钦、陈晓彬、蔡林华等被关押在看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月上旬，广东揭阳市榕城区法院在揭阳市判法轮功学员吴旭钦的母亲陈晓彬<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">陈晓红：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">山东胜利油田法轮功学员，女，二十三中的小学语文退休老师。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，滨海公安局基地分局大肆抓捕了二十多位法轮功学员，其中包括陈晓红。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，东营市东营区法院对陈晓红视频庭审，几天后宣判：陈晓红被判三年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚款两万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/3/24/458072.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/3/24/458072.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈新年：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河南南阳唐河县油田法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1947</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日陈新年、彭涛夫妇在南阳油田采油二厂，讲法轮功时，被不明真相的人诬告，被唐河县滨河派出所警察抓捕，被抄家，陈新年被关押在唐河县看守所。后家属被告知其已经被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，关押到郑州监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈秀芬：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广州市法轮功学员，女，广州市越秀区登峰小学退休教师，<span lang="EN-US">1954</span>年生。一九九九年炼法轮功。陈秀芬<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被警察破门入室抓捕、关押构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被广州市海珠区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚金一万元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/12/4_19.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/12/4_19.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> </span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈秀玲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东省潍坊寿光市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">60</span>多岁。陈秀玲曾于<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年被判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月再被抓捕，关押在山东省潍坊市看守所。在<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>～<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月间，陈秀玲被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/11/4_10.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/11/6/%E5%B1%B1%E4%B8%9C%E7%9C%81%E6%BD%8D%E5%9D%8A%E5%AF%BF%E5%85%89%E5%B8%82%E4%B8%89%E4%BD%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91-467924.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font:
