minor-fareast;">陈雪：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">福建省福州市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1975</span>年生，女，福建工程学院信息科学与工程学院教务员（原福建工程学院计算机与信息科学系教师），家住福建省福州市。她于<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月开始修炼法轮功。在中共对法轮功的疯狂迫害中，陈雪多次被中共迫害，曾被劳教两年，关押在福建省女子劳教所遭受迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日晚被福州市公安局晋安分局警察抓捕，关押在闽清看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，她被福州市马尾区法院庭审。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月获悉：陈雪女士被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/5/29/461396.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/5/29/461396.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈学远：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东青岛即墨区灵山街道东洼里后村村民、维权人士陈学远，人称“即墨老陈”，几乎每天都发布短视频，记录生活、曝光村里的贪腐问题。老陈的抖音账号（北京<span lang="EN-US">26</span>环）有<span lang="EN-US">4.7</span>万粉丝，被当地不少网友称作“农民反腐英雄”。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月底，他的抖音突然停止更新，之后得知他被青岛市公安局即墨分局拘留。律师提出变更强制措施申请，被拒绝。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，家属收到青岛市公安局即墨分局的逮捕通知书，得知陈学远疑被以涉嫌寻衅滋事罪名义逮捕，羁押在青岛市即墨看守所。据悉，陈学远在被抓前发布的短视频揭露了龙青高速公路建设给东洼里后村带来的水淹地问题、道路被破坏问题、遗留建筑物等问题。广大村民们纷纷联名为老陈喊冤。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/09/blog-post.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/09/blog-post.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">陈艳红：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">山东省青岛市城阳区法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1975</span>年生，女，家住青岛市城阳区惜福镇街道惜福镇小学校附近。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，城阳区公安分局闯入陈艳红家中将她强制抓捕到上马派出所，后警察抄家，将。她被抓捕的原因是她在发法轮功资料时，遭到不明真相的人恶意举报。陈艳红被抓捕后，一直在即墨普东看守所关押。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日被视频开庭、判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月被从即墨普东看守所转到山东省女子监狱迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/21/446559.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈跃飞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">天津市武清区河西务镇法轮功学员。女，家住天津市武清区河西务镇东西陈庄村。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日上午<span lang="EN-US">7</span>点多至<span lang="EN-US">10</span>点<span lang="EN-US">20</span>分左右，陈跃飞被闯入家中的河西务派出所警察抓捕、抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，被非法庭审。目前得知，陈跃飞女士于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年已被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈越利：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">香港基督徒，英文名<span lang="EN-US">Stephen</span>，陈越利（<span lang="EN-US">Stephen</span>）因参与基督教儿童主日学材料的印刷，于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日在西九龙海关被捕，并被控“非法经营罪”已正式逮捕。与他一同被拘捕的至少<span lang="EN-US">8</span>位以上基督徒。目前关押在湖北省咸宁赤壁市看守所，生死未卜、健康堪忧。<b>信息来源： <span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/01/stephen.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/01/stephen.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">陈银汝：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">江苏省苏州市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1954</span>年生。原驻苏州坦克十师三十八团营长、少校军官，转业后曾任中华联合财产保险公司任客户经理，一九九八年开始修炼法轮大法。陈银汝坚持法轮功、坚持给民众发放法轮功资料，多次被警察抓捕，先后四次被判刑。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，陈银汝在老家盐城市发放真相资料时遭人恶告，被当地警察抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月上旬，他被盐城市大丰区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚金一万元，已被关押到苏州监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;"> </span></b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/3/4/457391.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/3/4/457391.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈元华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">天津市宁河区法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1949</span>年生。陈元华自一九九八年开始修炼法轮大法。中共江泽民团伙疯狂迫害法轮功的<span lang="EN-US">20</span>多年中，陈元华有近一半的时间是被非法关押在看守所、洗脑班、劳教所、监狱，或者是在流离失所中度过。她多次被拘留、多次被关洗脑班，曾被非法劳教两年半，两次被判刑累计七年。因发法轮功资料于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被警察抓捕。后获知，陈元华老人被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，已于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月下旬被转监到天津女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/10/4_14.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/10/4_14.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">陈玉洁：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">锦州市凌海市金城镇法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日被抓捕、关押构陷，<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月被开庭，遭判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日被投入到辽宁省女子监狱继续关押。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="http://4.31.18.88/mh/articles/2022/3/12/%E8%BE%BD%E5%AE%81%E7%9C%81%E5%87%8C%E6%B5%B7%E5%B8%82%E9%99%88%E7%8E%89%E6%B4%81%E9%81%AD%E5%86%A4%E5%88%A4%E4%BA%94%E5%B9%B4%E5%85%A5%E7%8B%B1-439948.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">http://4.31.18.88/mh/articles/2022/3/12/%E8%BE%BD%E5%AE%81%E7%9C%81%E5%87%8C%E6%B5%B7%E5%B8%82%E9%99%88%E7%8E%89%E6%B4%81%E9%81%AD%E5%86%A4%E5%88%A4%E4%BA%94%E5%B9%B4%E5%85%A5%E7%8B%B1-439948.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈玉英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">北京市法轮功女学员。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月底，陈玉英被抓捕，一直被关押在顺义区看守所，有学员被密集提审并遭到背铐。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日获悉陈玉英被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。目前被关押在顺义区看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月底。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/10/716.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/10/716.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/9/30/%E5%8C%97%E4%BA%AC%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%B0%AD%E5%AE%88%E7%A4%BC%E3%80%81%E8%83%A1%E9%94%A6%E5%87%A4%E7%AD%89%E4%BA%94%E4%BA%BA%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91-466607.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/9/30/%E5%8C%97%E4%BA%AC%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%B0%AD%E5%AE%88%E7%A4%BC%E3%80%81%E8%83%A1%E9%94%A6%E5%87%A4%E7%AD%89%E4%BA%94%E4%BA%BA%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91-466607.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈云飞：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">1967</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日出生，四川省达州市达县人，个体农场主和农艺师，民主“业余驯兽师”，四川“民主行为艺术家”，著名维权公民、异议人士，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">1989</span>年曾参与过“<span lang="EN-US">89</span>学运”，六四镇压后返乡谋生，仍坚守民主理念，在当地展开多种帮助访民的维权活动，后因多次试图前往北京祭奠前中共总书记赵紫阳而被成都警方长期监控、威胁；<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，曾因在《成都晚报》刊登“向坚强的六四遇难者母亲致敬”的广告，被成都警方抓捕，后被以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”监视居住半年；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年，曾因以发起人名义与维权公民谭作人、冉云飞等捐血纪念六四而被警方警告、威胁；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年，曾因被怀疑参与“茉莉花革命”而被警方软禁家中多日；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，因不满和抗议当局禁止其出境旅行，而为其护照和港澳通行证举行别样葬礼，自此开中国此类葬礼之先河；同年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，曾因向四川省人大常委会递交“致习近平等先生的公开信”、“要求中国最有权力的<span lang="EN-US">205</span>名部级以上官员公开财产的公民建议书”以及<span lang="EN-US">7033</span>名有效公民的签名名单，而被拒绝签收；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，曾因租赁房屋被当局联合黑社会逼迁，搬迁中又遭遇暴徒的殴打和恶警的威胁攻击，终致其身体严重受损；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月至<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，又因其开通“成都市区到彭州中石化厂一日游旅游线路”而被当局忌恨，其活动随即被成都市警方搅局破坏。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，因其与维权公民<span lang="EN-US">20</span>余人到成都市新津县为当年的六四死难学生肖杰、吴国峰扫墓，遂在返程途中遭到上百名持枪特警的围追堵截，<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日即被四川省新津县警方以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”、“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，被以同罪名正式批捕。后检察院取消“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”，只以寻衅滋事罪起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日陈云飞被成都武侯区法院以“寻衅滋事罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日刑满释放。陈云飞于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>号晚上被</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">警察带走。<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日警察到他家里，将他的母亲送到了成都市温江区的侄儿家中。后获悉陈云飞被刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日下午，北京张磊律师在成都市陴都区看守所会见了陈云飞。陈云飞<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日被从陴都区的住处抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被以寻衅滋事罪名执行逮捕。陈云飞非常乐观，表示在看守所里一切都好，就像是换了一个地方工作，在哪里都可以帮助他人，都可以传福音，被关在看守所里的人更需要他传福音。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈云飞寻衅滋事案件已于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日移送成都市陴都区检察院审查起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，陈云飞昨被当局构陷获刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。中共法院官方通告如下：“<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，四川省成都市郫都区人民法院对被告人陈云飞强制猥亵、猥亵儿童一案依法不公开审理，并公开宣判，以被告人陈云飞犯强制猥亵罪，判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；犯猥亵儿童罪，判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年；数罪并罚，决定执行有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。”刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/12/4.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/12/4.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陈泽奇：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1963</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月出生，山西省太原市杏花岭区人，广东省深圳市龙岗区居民，深圳达特计算机公司软件开发部经理，计算机软件专家，法轮功信仰者，中国在押良心犯。在深圳从业<span lang="EN-US">20</span>余年，曾任职于多家公司的软件部负责人，为人谦和儒雅，工作成绩卓越，尤其是在深圳达特计算机公司软件开发部担任经理时，曾参与过多项软件开发，且主持研发的掌上电脑“一指禅”及“蓝精灵数码词典”是当时优秀的高新技术产品；但因信仰、宣传法轮功，而遭中共深圳当局强力打压；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，突然被深圳市龙岗区警方从家中抓捕刑拘，并被送往深圳市龙岗区看守所关押，其家遭查抄；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，被以涉嫌“邪教罪”转正式逮捕，指控其“系法轮功组织成员”，利用掌握的专业技术，组装伪基站给他人，并使用伪基站宣传法轮功，属违法行为；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，其案在深圳市龙岗区法院正式庭审，至<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，被深圳市龙岗法院一审以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，并罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；其不服上诉，后经深圳市中级人民法院二审裁决，依然维持原判，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。目前在广东省四会监狱服刑。</span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陈治坤：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广东五华县法轮功学员。男，<span lang="EN-US">1982</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月出生，重庆市铜梁区人，近年居住广东梅州市五华县。陈治坤于<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>年读高一时开始修炼法轮功，大学毕业后曾经在梁平县中学任高中教师。<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，他被重庆市梁平县（现梁平区）警察抓捕，被劳教一年。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年，陈治坤在浙江省散发神韵光盘与《九评共产党》等真相资料被警察抓捕；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，他被浙江省台州市路桥法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，梅州市五华县公安局警察抓捕了陈治坤，称他散发法轮功资料，并对他抄家。次日，陈治坤被刑事拘留；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，他被五华县检察院批准逮捕，后被梅县区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金三万。陈治坤上诉。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，梅州市中级法院驳回上诉，维持原判。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/09/26.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/09/26.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 123.75pt;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/9/21/%E5%B9%BF%E4%B8%9C%E4%BA%94%E5%8D%8E%E5%8E%BF%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E9%99%88%E6%B2%BB%E5%9D%A4%E3%80%81%E9%99%88%E6%A0%87%E5%AE%8F%E5%85%88%E5%90%8E%E9%81%AD%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4-465541.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-style: italic; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">陈忠国：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">四川省广汉市广兴镇法轮功学员。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">陈忠国<span lang="EN-US">1952</span>年生，退休工人，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>、<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月份被抓捕。陈忠国的妻子<span lang="EN-US">(</span>未修炼法轮功<span lang="EN-US">)</span>被抓捕到派出所暴打，暴力取证，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月陈忠国被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月。</span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">信息来源：</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/7/27/2022-7-27.html<o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">程贵芳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山西省阳泉市矿区法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年生。早年修炼法轮功，自<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月中共江泽民集团发动了对法轮功的迫害后，程贵芳因坚持真善忍信仰，长期遭中共人员迫害，被抓捕、关押、劳教、判刑。<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，被劳教一年。二零零九年被矿区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，关押在山西省女子监狱遭受迫害。程贵芳女士于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月被当地警察抓捕，被关押在看守所长达一年多后，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月才获悉，她已经被当地中共法院秘密判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，并已经被关押到山西省女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/12/3.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">程桂靖：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，天津市南开区法轮功学员，因信仰法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，程桂英、程桂靖姐妹被天津警方抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，程桂英、程桂靖被检察院批捕。<a name="_Hlk52179872">随后由南开分局预审科张伟以两人用手机打电话诉说法轮功学员被迫害事实真相为由，先后三次把构陷她们的材料上报南开检察院起诉，其中两次因证据不足退回。</a><span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，被南开法院判以重刑，并勒索高额罚金：程桂英被判<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年、勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">4</span>万元；程桂靖被判<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年、勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元。程桂英、程桂靖对判决提出上诉。天津第二中级法院驳回上诉，维持原判。家属被索要高额罚款。<a name="_Hlk52179802">关押在南开看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<b lang="EN-US">5</span>万元。程桂英、程桂靖对判决提出上诉。天津第二中级法院驳回上诉，维持原判。家属被索要高额罚款。</span></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">程来花</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：女，江西鹰潭市法轮功学员。家住鹰潭市月湖区建设路。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，程来花去余江县中童镇官坊程毛村清明扫墓，发放法轮功资料，遭余江县中童镇派出所抓捕、关押，后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，被关押在江西省女子监狱。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日下午，程来花因在火车站附近给人发了存有法轮功资料的优盘后，被警察抓捕到鹰潭市月湖区交通派出所，并被抄家。后程来花被关押在鹰潭市看守所。近日获悉，其已被鹰潭市贵溪市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New minor-fareast;">程连连：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日在发放法轮功资料时，遭八里湾镇派出所警察抓捕、关押。近日得知，程连连已被中共法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，张桂英被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。更多详情待查。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/5/10/442538.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/5/10/442538.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <o:p></o:p></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">程巧云：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黑龙江</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">大庆市采油九厂法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1960</span>年生，大庆管理局九龙实业公司物业分公司职工，家住大庆红岗区创业庄。早年修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年，中共江泽民集团迫害法轮功后，其屡遭抓捕和酷刑折磨。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日当天大庆警察抓捕了一百多名法轮功学员，程巧云也被抓捕，被关押在大庆第二看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月获悉，其被被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2030</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">。信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/2/6/456491.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/2/6/456491.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">程学珍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">湖北省武穴市法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1962</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月出生，现在被非法关押在黄冈市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日凌晨，武穴市公安局、田镇派出所、青林派出所、龙潭派出所同时出动，同一时间对郭平珍、龚月贵、刘艳峰、程学珍和廖元华五位法轮功学员的住宅、工作场所、法轮功学员及家人租借的房屋与仓库进行非法查抄，抄走法轮功书籍、资料、打印机、电脑等个人物品，并将五位法轮功学员抓捕，关押到看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，这五位法轮功学员被武穴市检察院非法批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，武穴市法院将五位法轮功学员判刑。郭平珍被判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元；龚月贵、刘艳峰和程学珍被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元；廖元华被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。程学珍刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">程玉兰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黑龙江</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">佳木斯法轮功学员。佳木斯市东风区建国乡群力村村民。一九九七年幸开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月中共开始对法轮功的残酷迫害后，程玉兰多次遭受迫害，曾经一度被迫流离失所、有家难回。程玉兰于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日被佳木斯前进公安分局国保大队入室抓捕、构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月被佳木斯向阳法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，罚金一万，于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被关押到黑龙江省女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/14/458788.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/14/458788.html</span></b></a></span><b><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">程渊：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">湖南省长沙市人，广东省深圳市常驻居民，中国民间公益机构“长沙富能”创办人（之一）、工作人员，乙肝病毒携带者、艾滋病病毒感染者等群体维权诉讼代理人，中国在押政治犯。因从事公益维权活动<span lang="EN-US">10</span>余年，曾代理过<span lang="EN-US">10</span>多起乙肝病毒携带者、艾滋病病毒感染者维权诉讼案，颇受弱势群体爱戴欢迎；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年，曾首例成功代理江西省进贤县艾滋就业歧视案，为当事人争得赔偿，经多家媒体报导而广为人知，但亦引起中共当局的高度警觉及跟踪监控；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，突然被湖南省长沙市国家安全局警方从深圳跨境带走，并被旋即以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”刑拘；审讯期间，被多次问及其在长沙富能所做的工作内容、资金来源及其近期外出活动（含去香港，与香港记者录像等）都做些什么等细节详情；据悉，被抓当天，其家属多受牵连，其妻竟被戴黑头套遭无辜审讯长达<span lang="EN-US">17</span>小时，其<span lang="EN-US">3</span>岁半幼女遭惊吓，夜晚睡觉出现抽搐和梦呓，白天表现惊恐异常，其兄程浩、其老父亲等均遭警告恐吓；其代理律师欲了解案件详情遭绝，仅告知其罪名及法定的拘留期限；<span lang="EN-US"> 2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，被长沙市国家安全局以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”转正式逮捕。后遭起诉，并被遭强行委派官派律师，对家属严密封锁，拒不见面。家属外界都无法获知案情进展。已经开庭审理，家属仍然对信息一无所知。被羁押于湖南省国家安全厅看守所。长沙富能发起人程渊的妻子施明磊综合各渠道信息，获悉长沙公益仨程渊、吴葛健雄、刘大志三人已在北京时间<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日上午被长沙市中级法院判决，吴葛健雄被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，刘大志被判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日获悉：长沙富能公益案之程渊被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年有期徒刑，</span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">现在于湖南赤山监狱服刑。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">程渊在赤山监狱被关禁闭三个月，强迫劳动暴瘦<span lang="EN-US">12</span>斤头发全白<span lang="EN-US">, </span>程渊家人收到家书伤心落泪<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">。</b></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="mso-tab-count: 1;"> </span><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/blog-post_98.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/blog-post_98.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/07/12.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/07/12.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">成梅花：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">广东省清远市连州市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1949</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月生，女。中专毕业，家住清远市连州市。她<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年开始修炼法轮功，因讲述法轮功被迫害的真相，她多次遭中共迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，她被清远市公安局劳教<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，被连州公安局拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日晚，成梅花在家中被连州警察抓捕，她的家被查抄，家里的法轮功书籍和资料被抄走。关押到连山拘留所；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，她被英德市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;"> </span></b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/7/447350.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/7/447350.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">褚新宇：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2018</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年，年过花甲的武汉人基督教阚小勇牧师携妻王凤英赴大连，创建门训家园网，传讲基督教。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，阚小勇牧师、王凤英夫妇突遭大连沙河口公安分局逮捕，同时被捕的还有四位教会女性同工褚新宇、赵乾娇、张松爱、梁冬芝，罪名是利用迷信破坏法律实施。而后甘井子区检察院又加增诈骗罪和非法经营罪，于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月诉至甘井子区院。一审庭审断续绵延近半年，总计开庭近<span lang="EN-US">30</span>天，于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>结束。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日获悉：大连基督教阚小勇牧师案一审判决结果已出炉。阚小勇牧师案阚小勇牧师判刑<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年、师母王凤英被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年、褚新宇被判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年。褚新宇刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2031</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/01/14410.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/01/14410.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">次成加材（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1986</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，西藏自治区那曲地区比如县人，又名次成坚参，笔名“秀真”，前四川甘孜州白玉佛学院僧人，前西北民族大学中文文学专业学生，西藏知名青年藏汉双语作家，中国在押政治犯。曾于<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年进入四川甘孜州白玉佛学院为僧，学习藏传佛教知识，截止<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年，曾先后在色达五明佛学院及德格协庆寺等多个寺庙进行过深造，并在此期间勤耕不缀，于<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年出版发行《雪域悲歌》、《雪域命运》等多部藏文著作；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年底还俗进入西北民族大学攻读中文文学写作专业，<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年在该大学与其他同学联合创办了《新一代》藏文杂志，担任主编，同时，他还在藏人文化网开设的“秀真博客”里，用中文撰写过多篇文章，其中著名的有《丑陋的拉萨》、《那一夜》、《那些年、那些事》等等；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，因其多次在大学里举办各种被政府视为非法主题的讨论会，触及了当局的敏感神经，随被当局开除学籍，同年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月返乡后又开办了一所业余学校，向家乡青年进行免费藏汉双语教学。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，由于比如县比如乡莫阿村、孟庆村和达塘乡等地发生多处藏人示威行动，以抗议当局强行开展“爱国再教育、家家挂红旗”的政治宣讲活动，故而被警方指控在县学校学生集体抗议和民众绝食示威等事件中有“煽动分裂国家”、“破坏社会稳定”、“公开发表非法言论”之嫌，遂于同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日被警方拘捕并抄家；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，又被西藏自治区高级法院以“煽动分裂国家罪”和“破坏社会稳定罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年。目前在西藏自治区拉萨市曲水监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">次成嘉措（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1982</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年出生，甘肃省甘南藏族自治州夏河县九甲乡人，夏河县拉卜楞寺僧人，藏族人权捍卫者，在押中国良心犯。自幼即进入拉卜楞寺为僧；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，因对中共当局高压严管制度的不满，甘肃省甘南州夏河县发生了大规模僧俗藏人的抗议游行，其亦参与其中；又因被当局视为带头抗议者，随在当局对抗议藏民展开大逮捕后被迫逃离；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，被甘南州警方在舟曲县抓捕刑拘，并送至甘肃省安全厅看守所关押，自此失联；<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，被甘南州中级法院一审以“分裂国家罪”秘密判处无期徒刑；其不服上诉，后经甘南州中级法院二审裁决，依然维持原判；</b>据悉，其在关押期间，曾惨遭刑讯逼供；从被捕至判刑以来，其私聘律师权、亲属探视权及到法庭旁听审判权均被拒绝；因其行为仅为以和平抗议方式来表达内心诉求，却遭司法枉法重判，故而随后又在夏河县城、拉卜楞寺院内外出现大量抗议传单。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年，次成嘉措获减刑，刑期减为<span lang="EN-US">19</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，又经甘肃省天水市中级法院批准，被二次减刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月获悉，其可能将于<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年刑满。目前疑似在甘肃省天水监狱（甘肃省天水市秦城区建设路<span lang="EN-US">196</span>号，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">741000</span>）服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/03/blog-post_27.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/03/blog-post_27.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">次旺嘉措：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1978</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，四川省甘孜藏族自治州新龙县人，藏名<span lang="EN-US">Tsewang Gyatso</span>，原甘孜藏族自治州新龙县塘吉乡（音译）小学厨师，中国在押政治犯。曾因积极参与罢耕运动和抵制中共控制的藏历新年庆祝活动，<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，被当局怀疑参与在该县塘吉乡（音译）境内的一起有关抗议中共暴政，散发传单、呼吁西藏独立的示威活动；事发当天因该抗议活动引发警民冲突，乡政府办公大楼发生火灾，随于<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日被新龙县警方强行抓捕，并被以涉嫌“煽动分裂国家罪”和“扰乱社会秩序罪”刑事拘留，关押于四川省成都市某看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被四川省甘孜州中级法院以“煽动分裂国家”和“扰乱社会秩序”两项罪名判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">16</span>年。目前在四川省德阳市黄许镇德阳监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">仓央嘉措（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">出生年月不详，西藏自治区那曲人，藏族僧人，那曲地区索县赤多乡珍达寺（又称直达寺）诵经师、财务主管，中国在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，因中共当局发现西藏那曲地区索县有人利用手机和微信传播所谓 “禁止材料”（如转发印有达赖喇嘛的图片、传播涉及民族尊严的歌曲及透露被封锁的地方消息等），且在围墙上喷涂“西藏独立”等字样，遂展开大规模抓捕行动；<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日—<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，多名当地僧侣及村民被当局以莫须有罪名拘捕，多数人长期下落不明，仓央嘉措亦于<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被当地警方从寺庙驻地抓走，后以涉嫌“与境外联系”及“煽动他人反政府”罪由刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，被当局以“向外界保持联络”和“鼓励该寺年轻僧人反抗中国政府活动”等罪名重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年。目前被羁押于西藏自治区拉萨市曲水监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">丛兰英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">山东省威海市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1945</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年已经<span lang="EN-US">78</span>岁。丛兰英老人<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日下午<span lang="EN-US">5</span>点多，在家中被威海市环翠区公安分局国保警察抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，丛兰英被荣成市法院以所谓的“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，并两万元罚款。目前，丛兰英被关押在文登看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/5/458482.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/5/458482.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">丛霞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">大连法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，丛霞外出贴法轮功材料，被大连西岗区国保大队和西岗区八一路派出所抓捕。后丛霞被构陷到大连西岗区检察院，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月被庭审，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月上诉，<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月二审被维持冤判。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月初，辽宁大连法轮功学员丛霞被从大连看守所转至沈阳女子监狱，因大连疫情原因，至今不许探视。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/11/26/%E5%A4%A7%E8%BF%9E%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E4%B8%9B%E9%9C%9E%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4-434060.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/11/26/%E5%A4%A7%E8%BF%9E%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E4%B8%9B%E9%9C%9E%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4-434060.html</span></b></a></span><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">楚继东：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">（又名褚继东）<span lang="EN-US">1975</span>年生，原天津市大港油田法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，中共开始疯狂迫害法轮功后，楚继东进京和平请愿，被劳教<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年；因他坚持信仰，再被劳教<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，再加期<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，那就是<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，又连续被关押到天津多个劳教所迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年获悉，其在流落到宁夏后被抓捕，遭到残酷迫害，楚继东绝食抵制迫害至少有<span lang="EN-US">90</span>多天。据悉已被判刑<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年，其他情况待查。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2035</span>年。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源： </b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/5/3/442030.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/5/3/442030.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">崔斌：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">重庆维权人士。崔斌早在<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年，因见义勇为，帮助消防武警官兵救人时，膝盖被武警踩伤，从而造成二级伤残。但重庆市政府不仅不依法承认他的见义勇为行为，更不按照相关法律政策给予奖励和救助，在万般无奈之下，他被迫走上了上访之路。期间，多次遭到重庆维稳部门删帖封号、监视居住、非法拘禁、拘留、殴打等一系列迫害。由此，崔斌由一位访民，逐渐成长为一名民主维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年因在北京二中院围观浦志强案而被抓进久敬庄，被关押五天。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年参与声援郭飞雄签名活动，并在高笋塘步行街广场公开绝食以示声援，再遭传唤。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月两会期间，崔斌因在北京拦截两会代表车辆，在重庆驻京办被关了<span lang="EN-US">5</span>天黑监狱。之后被地方警察押送回家，再遭万州警方<span lang="EN-US">"</span>监视居住<span lang="EN-US">"</span>软禁一年。期间因外出没有事前“报告”，被行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天。当地维稳部门一直是崔斌为“眼中钉肉中刺”。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日崔斌就曾遭受过一次黑社会人员的殴打，那次是因为他进京上访，被重庆维稳部门所忌恨，于是他们指使黑社会人员用杀猪刀砍断了他双手的八根筋健和三根手指骨，并且全身多处被暴打砍伤。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，崔斌背着写有“孙政才独裁暴政腐化之风还在重庆漫延，重庆人民生活在水生火热之中”的牌子在高笋塘步行街广场游行，之后又穿着印有“当人民恐惧政府即为暴政”文化衫拍照并在网上传播，又遭传唤抄家。崔斌的处境日益艰难。长期以来，崔斌一直在当地警方的严密监控中，并被以各种方式，限制或变相限制其人身自由，尤其外出受到更明显的限制。崔斌自<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日突然失联，后获悉：崔斌为自卫杀了维稳警察派去迫害他的黑帮人员，后遭刑事拘留。先是关押在重庆万州看守所。后获悉崔斌遭到起诉判刑，一直关押在重庆万州看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，重庆维权公民前往万州看守所给崔斌上账<span lang="EN-US">,</span>遭到拒绝，后经询问得知崔斌已被判死缓，已由重庆万州看守所转到重庆蜀都监狱关押。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">崔兵：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁省葫芦岛市南票区法轮功学员，</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1963</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日早上五点左右，南票新区季家屯沿海派出所四五个警察闯入崔兵家，没有出示搜查证，就抄家，并抓捕了崔兵，没有开被抄走的物品清单。崔兵被关押在葫芦岛看守所。此次抓捕是因为上次<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日晚九点钟，崔兵等人去南票区高桥镇朱家洼村发真相资料。被村民恶意举报，那次是因为疫情，被放回。后其被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/3/3/457359.html#2332214919-18"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/3/3/457359.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">崔长胜：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江哈尔滨市阿城区法轮功学员。崔长胜曾于<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，崔长胜与母亲张丽华被当地警察抓捕；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月他们分别被阿城区法院判刑五年、六年。崔长胜被劫持到呼兰监狱迫害，他母亲张丽华被劫持到黑龙江省女子监狱迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日早晨，被阿城区公安局和阿城区金城派出所多名警察，入室抓捕崔长胜，在没通知家属的情况下开庭，被阿城区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，几个月后家属才得到消息。现在崔长胜被关押在阿城区第一看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;"> </span></b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/5/25/461269.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/5/25/461269.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东省东营市东营法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，东营市公安局、分局、市国保支队、区国保大队及六户派出所、胜利派出所、新区派出所实施了抓捕，当时共有包括王霞、崔桂芬、王沐怡在内的十多名法轮功学员被抓捕、抄家。其中，王霞因身体原因，被“取保候审”，崔桂芬、王沐怡两人被关押于东营市看守所。山东省东营市东营区法院于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日对王霞、崔桂芬、王沐怡进行开庭宣判。法官闫晓辉在没有任何法律依据的情况下对她们作出了非法判决。王霞被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚款两万五千元；崔桂芬被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，罚款两万元；王沐怡被判<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚款一万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。</span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/3/2022-3-3.html#zip4"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">崔建秀：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">山东日照法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1961</span>年生。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">日照市莒县小店镇薛家孟堰村人，崔建秀是<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日在夏庄镇给一位清洁工一份真相资料后，被夏庄镇中共党委干部岳青海恶意举报，被夏庄镇派出所不法警察抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月上旬，在北京律师做出有理有据的无罪辩护情况下，山东省日照市五莲县法院仍旧判崔建秀<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年有期徒刑。崔建秀不服判决，已上诉。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/24/2022-3-24.html#zip3"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/24/2022-3-24.html#zip3</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">崔兰琴：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河北省任丘市吕公堡乡法轮功学员，吕公堡乡辛安庄村人。崔兰琴<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日在北村讲真相，告诉人们瘟疫中如何自救，被吕公堡派出所巡警绑架。崔兰琴被关押在看守所，据悉于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日开庭。崔兰琴女儿在过年前给辩护律师打电话得知，她的妈妈被判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">崔荣：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁省辽阳市法轮功学员。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2021</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被抓捕，被关押在辽阳市看守所。后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/5/21/461085.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/5/21/461085.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">崔太：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1950 </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，又名崔泰，圣名奥斯定（<span lang="EN-US">Agostino Cui Tai</span>），河北省张家口市人，天主教徒，河北省张家口市宣化教区主教，有“献祭的羔羊”之称，中国在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年，曾在河北保定修道院培育后而晋铎（即类似于职位晋升），并由河北省易县教区师恩祥主教祝圣（即任命主教的一种仪式）为神父；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年，又被梵蒂冈天主教教宗本笃十六世任命为河北省张家口市宣化教区的助理主教，协助主教赵克勋（<span lang="EN-US">Tommaso Zhao Kexun</span>）的神职工作；然而，正是基于其对国际正统天主教的认知和竭力在教会里牧养教友，虽被教会同工及教友们共认为是一位生活简朴，严于律己，充满圣德的好牧者，并被誉为“献祭的羔羊”，但却因不愿认同中共政权控制下的天主教爱国教会的权威性，随受打压和迫害；曾被当局多次非法拘押，并遭软禁和被强迫旅游累计长达<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年；拘押期间，曾因拒不说出有关宣化教区主教赵克勋的确切信息（含<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年赵去世后的埋葬地址）而惨遭酷刑；后因长期被羁押，河北省当局从<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年起，准许其在中国农历新年及中秋节等重要节日，可获暂时假释回家数天，然而在复活节之前又会再被警方带走，或被要求送到指定的关押地点；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，其因农历春节将至而被暂时获释回家，但时逢疫情大流行，其须与家人共处到<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月才能返回；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，其被张家口市宣化区警方突然再次抓捕刑拘，罪名不清；失联至今，一直不被释放；后获悉，其此次被抓皆因之前曾发布过三份文告，并公开自己是被罗马教廷承认的主教身份，但此主教身份却不被中共当局接受，故其公开主教身份的行为则被视为违法。目前被羁押地点不明。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/06/blog-post_2.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/06/blog-post_2.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">崔艳玲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吉林省延边州法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1957</span>年生，原吉林省延边州和龙市石棉水泥制品厂主管会计，<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月开始修炼法轮法轮功。崔艳玲女士因邮寄法轮功真相信，于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日被长春市公安局朝阳分局红旗街派出所警察入室抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月被长春市朝阳区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被关押到吉林省女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/7/30/%E9%82%AE%E5%AF%84%E7%9C%9F%E7%9B%B8%E5%8A%9D%E5%96%84%E4%BF%A1-%E5%90%89%E6%9E%97%E5%BB%B6%E8%BE%B9%E5%B4%94%E8%89%B3%E7%8E%B2%E9%81%AD%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E5%85%A5%E7%8B%B1-463586.html"><b mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河北省衡水市景县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1961</span>年生，退休职工。她的丈夫孟凡胜，六十岁，退伍军人，家住河北省衡水市景县。夫妇俩在北京帮助儿子看孩子。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，孟凡胜和崔永芬夫妇在北京海淀区一小区内照看四岁的孙子，发放法轮功真相卡片，被人恶意举报，遭跟踪。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日上午，崔永芬和孟凡胜在他们的儿子家被北京市海淀区公安分局和田村路派出所警察抓捕，被抄家，被关押到北京海淀看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，孟凡胜被释放，回到在北京的儿子家。崔永芬继续被关押在北京海淀区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月崔永芬被北京海淀区山后法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，罚金三千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/9/6/448758.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">杜荣、杜艳红、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">杜振田、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">杜志俊</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">段守珍、段宜法、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">多吉扎西（藏）、多杰扎才（藏）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">达吾提汗﹒达尔古色孜（哈萨克）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1973</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，新疆博尔塔拉蒙古自治州温泉县人，哈萨克族，博尔塔拉蒙古自治州温泉县牧民，人权捍卫者。自<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日起，新疆博尔塔拉蒙古自治州温泉县先后有<span lang="EN-US">30</span>多哈萨克族人（不分年龄、职业，甚至有年轻学生及政府公务员等）因“在微信群里，讨论如何移民哈萨克斯坦国”事宜被中共当局抓捕，其亦因关注移民事宜，并积极协助哈萨克村民移民哈萨克斯坦而在此次当局大抓捕中遭受迫害；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月突然被博尔塔拉蒙古自治州温泉县警方以涉嫌“危害国家安全罪”传唤、刑拘，后很快被温泉县检察院正式批捕，被指“帮人移民到哈萨克斯坦”就是犯了严重的政治问题。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月被博尔塔拉蒙古自治州温泉县法院一审以“危害国家安全罪”秘密重判<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年。其不服，已提起上诉。据悉，羁押期间曾惨遭酷刑毒打，病危住院，但出院后仍被立即重判，其要求聘请辩护律师也被拒绝。目前被羁押于新疆博尔塔拉蒙古自治州温泉县看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">达日（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州阿坝县人，藏族牧民，人权捍卫者。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，他与赞查（藏）二人皆因“为达赖喇嘛八十寿辰祈寿案”而被阿坝县警方拘捕，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州中级法院以不详罪名分别重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，据悉，当局拒绝其聘请代理律师为其辩护。目前关押服刑地点不详。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">代群英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">四川省泸州市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1952</span>年生，纸箱厂退休职工，家住泸州市江阳区国窖社区。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，代群英等<span lang="EN-US">4</span>名法轮功学员到合江县自怀镇赶场时被抓捕，随后被批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，被关押<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多的<span lang="EN-US">4</span>名法轮功学员被合江法院判刑，其中代群英被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">7</span>千元，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被关押到成都龙泉女子监狱四监区迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p
