mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">戴耀廷：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1964</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日出生，英语名：<span lang="EN-US">BennyTai Yiu-ting</span>，香港人，基督徒，香港法律学者，前香港大学法律学院副院长和副教授，“占中三子”，民主派意见领袖，中国在押政治犯。自幼生长于香港；<span lang="EN-US">1980</span>年代，中学毕业后曾就读于香港大学法律系，获取法律学士学位后，又取得法律深造证书，并在英国伦敦大学获得法律硕士学位；早年曾有浓烈的“中国情怀”，喜读中文和中国历史，后在大学期间，因吸收民主自由思想而认识到一国之强大不只是富国强兵，而是让它走向宪政，遂研究兴趣转为宪法、宪政、公法、法律和政治及宗教的关系、人权及参与式民主等，并成为民主派意见领袖；大学毕业后，曾在民主派领袖李柱铭办公担任法案助理，并是《香港基本法咨询委员会》两位学生代表之一，同时对“一国两制”的实施提出了批判与质疑；之后曾多年在香港大学法律系当副教授、并曾在<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-2008</span>年期间担任法律学院副院长；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年，曾因提出“让爱与和平占领中环”观念而闻名，并认为香港若未能有“真正普选”，即应该参与占领行动以争取<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年香港行政长官选举得以有“真正选择”；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月、<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月、<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年，曾因先后提出雷动计划、风云计划及民主派<span lang="EN-US">35+</span>初选等行动，而赢得香港市民的极大支持和响应，但却屡遭亲共建制派人士及媒体攻击。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年，随着港版国安法的正式实施，其很快被香港国安警方拘捕，被控曾因发起“占领中环”运动，并于<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日<span lang="EN-US">-28</span>日在香港中环金钟不同地点“煽惑他人”或“煽惑他人煽惑”非法阻碍行车道，因而被捕；同年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，其被西九龙裁判法院庭审裁决“串谋犯公众妨扰罪”和“煽惑他人犯公众妨扰罪”罪名成立；至<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，被判监<span lang="EN-US">16</span>个月；其不服判决，提起上诉，并申请保释；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，在服刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月后，终被获准以<span lang="EN-US">10</span>万港元保释等候上诉，并要交出旅游证件，不可离开香港；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日<span lang="EN-US">-26</span>日其上诉在香港高级法院被聆讯；同年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，其保释被撤回而返监；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，其上诉最终被驳回；同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，其副教授一职被香港大学校委会以在“占领中环”运动中有“不当行为”为由解聘，同期，其与另外二人又被廉政公署以在<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年协调民主派初选时涉嫌选举开支非法行为等为罪由起诉；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，被香港区域法院又以“串谋颠覆国家政权罪”等罪名判囚<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月；并与之前罪刑同期执行；截至目前，其等多人涉嫌民主派初选案，因系漫长而系列的审讯，故其仍需在押，继续候审。目前在香港大屿山石壁监狱服刑。</span><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/09/blog-post_69.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/09/blog-post_69.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">戴之颖：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">上海法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1956</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">66</span>岁，家住上海市普陀区新村路。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日中共发动对法轮功的疯狂迫害后，因坚持信仰，她一直被中共当局监控、跟踪、上门骚扰等，被迫离家出走。<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，她在山东被抓捕，后被劫持回上海，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，在上海松江女子监狱遭受迫害，<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月出狱。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，戴之颖被河南洛阳警方跨省抓捕，当日晚戴之颖被河南洛阳警方劫持离开上海，关押在河南洛阳市。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，戴之颖被判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚款<span lang="EN-US">4</span>万元。她家中有<span lang="EN-US">88</span>岁老母亲（也是法轮功学员），现在独居在家。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2030</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;"> <span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/2/445670.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/2/445670.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">丹增曲培（藏）</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>年出生，西藏自治区那曲市色尼区达前乡人，西藏知名企业家、慈善家，藏语言文化及生态环境保护者，藏人民生问题关切者，藏族人权捍卫者，在押中国政治犯。近年来，作为一名杰出的藏族企业家，因常年致力于保护藏语言文化和生态环境，促进藏人的团结意识，以及将自己的收入捐给慈善事业等，故而深受各地藏人的称赞和尊重；但也正因如此，却被中共西藏当局视为需要极度关注和严控防范的异己对象；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，当其从四川省成都市出差返回西藏拉萨时，在拉萨贡嘎机场突遭拉萨警方围堵与拦截，并就其携带私人物品及其住宅进行搜查；后因发现其存有一些与政治有关的书籍和一副达赖喇嘛的法相，遂被强制带走，自此失踪；后知其在被单独拘押<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多之久后，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，被西藏自治区拉萨市中级法院以“煽动分裂国家罪”、“非法向境外发送情报罪”和“资助危害国家安全活动罪”等多罪枉法重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">18</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，并没收所有个人财产；其不服，提起上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，经西藏自治区高级法二审裁决，依然维持原判，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2037</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。目前在拉萨市曲水监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/08/18.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/08/18.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">邓芳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">广东省广州市法轮功学员。曾兴阳妻子，<span lang="EN-US">1977</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月出生，湖南省衡阳市人，大学毕业，在培训机构任职。曾兴阳、妻子邓芳、妹妹曾跃玲，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日被天河区公安分局国保和石牌派出所警察抓捕，关押到天河区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，海珠区法院对<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人判刑，曾兴阳被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，被勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；邓芳被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，被勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">6</span>千元；曾跃玲被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，被勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">6</span>千元。邓芳刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/11/447538.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/11/447538.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">邓光英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">重庆访民，被强制关押精神病医院。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日晚<span lang="EN-US">23</span>点邓光英在北京市丰台区吕村被朱家坟派出所抓捕至今，邓光英的家人至今没有收到任何拘押通知。邓光英父亲还透露，地方政府的官员曾多次上门，要求在邓光英属于精神病人的材料上签字。对地方政府的无理要求，邓光英的父亲予以断然拒绝。一个没有任何精神病症状的正常人，只不过因为信访反映问题与争取自身权益，表达诉求，就属于精神病人，就要拘禁于精神病院，这就是社会主义官僚的固有思维，然而用践踏国家法律与公民人权的方式。至<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月仍被精神病，未释放。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; tab-stops: 122.5pt; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">邓国行</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：河南商水县法轮功学员。男，<span lang="EN-US">1950</span>年代生人，河南商水县姚集乡白茬村人。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月中旬去街上买馍时跟民众讲法轮功，遭人恶告，被警察抓捕到商水拘留所，<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天后被劫持到商水看守所关押。当时邓国行拒绝所谓“转化”，警察说：不转化永远不让出去。邓国行绝食反迫害，要求无条件放人。警察又利用灌食方式迫害邓国行。邓国行被关押<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多后，被判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，被关押在郑州新密监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/4/%E6%B2%B3%E5%8D%97%E5%95%86%E6%B0%B4%E5%8E%BF%E6%9D%A8%E6%98%A5%E6%A2%85%E3%80%81%E9%82%93%E5%9B%BD%E8%A1%8C%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E5%85%A5%E7%8B%B1-434357.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/4/%E6%B2%B3%E5%8D%97%E5%95%86%E6%B0%B4%E5%8E%BF%E6%9D%A8%E6%98%A5%E6%A2%85%E3%80%81%E9%82%93%E5%9B%BD%E8%A1%8C%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E5%85%A5%E7%8B%B1-434357.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">邓洪成：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1967</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，湖南省岳阳市人，网名“成主民”，微博名“湘人血性”，自由职业者，广东省深圳市龙岗区阪田街杨美东四巷<span lang="EN-US">9</span>号租住户，深圳同城聚会公民，民主宪政追求者，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，因邓洪成与肖兵、王威、李南海等多人在深圳市五和餐厅聚餐，席间李南海与肖兵被陌生人拍照（事后得知是国保），<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日中午，深圳市警方前往餐厅调查，手拿李南海、肖兵的照片要求工作人员指认，当天午后邓洪成与深圳维权公民肖兵、沈力、李南海、王威被警方扣押，自此失联；其侄子邓剑峰与同城聚餐公民丁岩、董凌鹏、王军及等得知消息之后前往其住处（深圳市杨美村五巷）寻找，亦遭失联；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，其在江西的家属被当地派出所警察查问，且拒绝透露当邓洪成下落及具体情况；后获知，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，其叔侄二人被深圳市警方以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”执行指定居所监视居住，其侄子邓剑锋后被取保候审释放；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，邓洪成被深圳市检察院以同罪名正式批捕。目前被羁押于深圳市第二看守所。后获悉，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日获刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年有期徒刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">邓静静<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">北京法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，邓静静等<span lang="EN-US">13</span>名法轮功修炼者被北京警方抓捕，包括邓静静在内的<span lang="EN-US">11</span>位被指控“破坏法律实施罪”。<span lang="EN-US">11</span>人被逮捕起诉涉及在疫情期间发布一些国内疫情照片及与其法轮功修炼者的身份有关。邓静静被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/20/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-437033.html<o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">邓天玉：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖北省荆州市沙市区法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1950</span>年生。因修炼法轮功，她曾经在<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年被抓捕、判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，在武汉女子监狱遭受残忍酷刑折磨，双手背铐、用四根绳子吊在房梁上脚尖落地七天七夜，被药物迫害一度精神失常。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日上午十点左右，邓天玉老人在发法轮功资料时被沙市区<span lang="EN-US">610</span>抓捕到荆州市沙市区解放派出所，下午五点多钟才回家。邓天玉被监视居住，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日又被沙市区解放派出所抓捕，直接送往石首市（县级市）隔离，于<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日晚上从石首市转入荆州区第一看守所，关押至今。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月又被秘密判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，家属都不知道到底几时开的庭，几时宣判的。这是邓天玉老太太第三次被判刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">邓万英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川泸州市法轮功学员。罗太会、雷焕英、邓万英、苟正琼，家住泸州市龙马潭区特兴镇。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日晚<span lang="EN-US">8</span>点，苟正琼在泸县兆雅镇给学生讲真相时，遭兆雅镇派出所警察抓捕。同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，又在泸州市龙马潭区特兴镇，抓捕了正在各自店铺里工作的法轮功学员邓万英、雷焕英、罗太会。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月得知，被关押了两年的泸州市龙马潭区特兴镇<span lang="EN-US">4</span>名法轮功学员罗太会、雷焕英、邓万英，苟正琼，因为信仰法轮大法，在<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次庭审后，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月上旬，被泸县法院判刑：邓万英<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，雷焕英<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罗太会<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，苟正琼<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。邓万英刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/4/%E5%9B%9B%E5%B7%9D%E6%B3%B8%E5%B7%9E%E5%B8%82%E5%9B%9B%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%89%E8%87%B3%E4%B9%9D%E5%B9%B4-430406.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/4/%E5%9B%9B%E5%B7%9D%E6%B3%B8%E5%B7%9E%E5%B8%82%E5%9B%9B%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%89%E8%87%B3%E4%B9%9D%E5%B9%B4-430406.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">邓秀芬<span lang="EN-US">: </span></span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">梁顺景妻子。梁顺景<span lang="EN-US">:1961</span>年出生，广东省梅州市梅县区城东镇人，原中国工商银行梅州分行职工，梅州城区江南团结路苏泊尔电器店负责人，法轮功信仰者。因为人谦和、厚道而深受他人好评；又因其与其妻邓秀芬在当地共同承办苏泊尔电器店（主营电器厨器专卖批发），生意上注重诚实守信，随其公司至<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年底时已有较大发展；但因梁顺景、邓秀芬夫妇<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人在信仰追求上笃信并积极宣传法轮功，随遭广东省梅州市当局的强力打压；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，其夫妇<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人在开车外出讲解宣传法轮功时，被事先蹲坑等候的梅州市梅江区警方及“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”管理办公室人员联合抓走，其家遭查抄，当场搜走法轮功书籍多套、计算机、打印机及银行卡、身份证等个人对象（如）多件，并将其日用汽车也拉走扣留；次日，其妻因血压高达<span lang="EN-US">180/230</span>，让家人暂时接回，其本人则被梅江区警方以涉嫌邪教罪刑拘，关押至梅江区芹黄看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，其夫妇<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人被梅江区检察院以同罪名正式批捕；同年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，其案在梅州市梅江区法院开庭审理；虽因该法院违反法定诉讼程序，其辩护律师曾据理要求法院重新开庭审判，但其与其妻仍然被该法院<span lang="EN-US">1</span>审以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”枉法重判；其中，梁顺景被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，其妻邓秀芬被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，并各处罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元；其<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人不服，均提起上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，经广东省梅州市中级法院二审裁决，依然维持原判；其刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，其妻邓秀芬刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日；据悉，其在看守所时被查出身体长有<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个肿瘤，在被庭审时其辩护权及辩护律师执业权被剥夺；其承办的苏泊尔电器店因长时无人经营，故被迫关门。目前在广东省<span lang="EN-US">4</span>会监狱（广东省<span lang="EN-US">4</span>会市济广塘镇<span lang="EN-US">/</span>广东省肇庆市<span lang="EN-US">4</span>会监狱<span lang="EN-US">290</span>信箱，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">526237</span>）服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">邓燕祥：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1980</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年代出生，广东省人，佛山市顺德区公民，基督徒，基督教全职侍奉同工，广东顺德盛佳家庭教会传道人，中国在押良心犯。早期曾为经商人，后因皈依基督教而将精力和爱好全心转投到教会的各项服侍活动中；又因为人和善、待人极有爱心，故其在顺德盛佳教会全职服侍的<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年间，曾帮助过许多对面临婚姻解体的基督徒夫妻，深得教会同工及教友信任与喜爱；但自近年来，因中共当局加强了对宗教事务条例的管理及修订，其所在盛佳教会频繁被当地民宗局要求加入和接受中共所属的“三自教会”的管理，被其等多次拒绝，遂屡被地方民宗局及顺德区警方的上门骚扰和警告；<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，盛佳教会突遭顺德区警方、民宗局和小区人员等数十人的连手冲击，教会使用的计算机、桌椅及教学物品等被翻查，教会大门被查封，邓燕祥、朱龙江、王伟才、朱巧玲<span lang="EN-US">4</span>名教会同工被警方带走；次日（<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日），其<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人均被顺德区警方以涉嫌“非法经营罪”刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，邓燕祥等<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人又被佛山市顺德区检察院以同罪名正式批捕，指控其等因让信徒使用教会印刷的内部学习数据，而此行为和思想意识与国家新修订的宗教管理条例相违背，故应予以逮捕、法办；被抓捕至今，其等均无更多具体信息，只知其等家属及孩子的生活、工作和上学正面临极大压力，教会其余未抓捕的同工和信徒仍遭警方持续传唤约谈；据悉，教会信徒均表示，因他们参与的家庭教会受到中国“宗教自由白皮书”保护，故而教会自己印刷内部学习数据并不违法。目前被羁押于佛山市南海区看守所（广东省佛山市南海区狮山镇招大（管理区）兴业东路，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">528200</span>）。信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/06/blog-post_28.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/06/blog-post_28.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/07/blog-post_56.html</span></b></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">迪克坦开（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1985</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年出生，甘肃省甘南州夏河县拉卜楞寺僧人。藏族人权捍卫者，在押中国良心犯。次成嘉措、迪克坦开两位拉卜楞寺僧人因与<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日在夏河县发生的大规模僧俗民众的抗议游行，随后被抓捕。次成嘉措被认为是带头抗议者，在当局对抗议藏人展开大逮捕后出逃，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日于舟曲县遭捕。迪克坦开也于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年遭捕。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，被甘南州中级法院一审以“分裂国家罪”秘密判处<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年有期徒刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2034</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">迪力夏提·吾力拜依：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1962</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日出生，新疆维吾尔自治区伊犁哈萨克自治州奎屯市人，哈萨克族名 <span lang="EN-US">Dilshat Oralbai</span>，穆斯林，曾先后任新疆伊犁日报社、伊犁州政治协会、奎屯日报社记者、作家、翻译员、文学总编辑等，哈萨克斯坦国创办企业总负责人，著名新疆媒体人，中国在押良心犯。自<span lang="EN-US">1985</span>年大学毕业起至<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年，曾先后在伊犁日报社、伊犁州政治协会、奎屯日报社工作，担任记者、作家、翻译员、文学总编辑等职务；曾翻译出版、发行<span lang="EN-US">15</span>部文学书籍（含儒勒·凡尔纳的《格兰特船长的儿女》等）、<span lang="EN-US">30</span>余本短篇小说（如《自由》等）及<span lang="EN-US">3</span>部电视剧等，并有<span lang="EN-US">10</span>多篇文章在新疆地区多次获奖；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年—<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年，曾到国外创业，并在哈萨克斯坦国开办企业，自认企业负责人，创办生产塑料窗框和房门的工厂；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年，因听从中共新疆政府要求在外哈萨克族人必须回国，遂与两个妹妹纷纷返回国内；起初两年生活安然如常，<span lang="EN-US">2018 </span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，迪力夏提·吾力拜依与两个妹妹突然被伊犁州奎屯市警方以不知名罪由抓捕，并送某政治再教育转化营关押，自此失联；<span lang="EN-US"> 2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，其家属接到警方口头通知，知其被伊犁哈萨克自治州奎屯市法院以不确罪名判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">25</span>年，其两个妹妹亦遭同等命运，大妹被判<span lang="EN-US">19</span>年，小妹被判<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年； 据悉，其因曾做过<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次手术，身体极度虚弱需要及时服药，但在狱中却遭虐待，狱方不仅让其从早到晚不停工作，且拒绝对其进行应有的基本治疗；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2043</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月。目前在新疆生产建设兵团农七师奎屯监狱（新疆伊犁哈萨克自治州奎屯市，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">833200</span>）服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">丁汉忠</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：<span lang="EN-US">1961</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日出生，山东省潍坊市昌乐县乔官镇丁家山村村民，退伍军人，抗暴维权者。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年因其住宅遭强拆而引发房屋权属争议，双方未达成拆迁安置补偿协议，后其房屋虽被当局非法偷拆和强拆过两次，但因其誓死捍卫，屡次报警，并到镇县政府多次反映逼拆问题而终使家园得以保全，遂引起当地官员的极端仇视。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日其房屋被进行第三次强拆，因来势凶猛，言行蛮横恶劣，差点使其和家人被砸在屋内，随引起冲突，其全家遭暴打群殴，其头颅前部被拆迁方严重铲伤，当即血流如注，头昏眼花。其曾先后<span lang="EN-US">5</span>次报警，但警方却迟迟未到，情急之下其被迫自卫，致使<span lang="EN-US">2</span>名暴力拆迁者受伤，后经抢救无效死亡。其亦因头部伤势过重被送进医院抢救，但很快被赶来的昌乐县警方逮捕。审讯期间，惨遭酷刑折磨。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日其被山东潍坊中级法院以“故意杀人罪”判处死刑，剥权终身。其不服上诉。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日经山东省高院二审，要求撤销一审判决，发回重审。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日再审，最终被以“故意杀人罪”改判为死缓。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，二审维持原判。目前被羁押在潍坊市昌乐县看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">丁家喜：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1967</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日出生，湖北省宜昌市人，前沈阳航空工业总公司、北京航空工业总公司工程师，曾任职北京律师协会企业重组专业委员会委员，中国民主同盟中央法制委员会委员，北航创业家协会秘书长，中关村国际孵化软件协会法律委员会主任等，原德鸿律师事务所主任，著名人权律师，北京新公民运动的组织者和协调人之一，中国在押政治犯。自<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年起，曾因积极参与推动“随迁子女就地高考”的教育平权活动，<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，又与许志永、孙含会、王永红等人发表致新任中共中央总书记习近平等中共高层领导人公开信，要求包括习近平在内的<span lang="EN-US">205</span>名中国部级以上官员率先财产公示，并广泛征集公民联署超过八千余人。这些活动触动了中共脆弱敏感的神经，遂于<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被北京警方以“非法集会”罪刑事拘留，关押于北京市第三看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日和<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，北京警方又先后将其罪名改换为“寻衅滋事罪”和“聚众扰乱社会秩序罪”；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，被北京当局以“聚众扰乱社会秩序罪”开庭审案，但鉴于法院在审判中出现严重违法现象，对案件结果明显不利，故其不得不当庭宣布解除对辩护律师的委托，迫使法院只得宣布休庭，择日宣判；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，经北京市海淀区法院再次重审，终被以“聚众扰乱公共场所秩序罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，后送往天津市茶淀站前进监狱服刑；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，刑满释放；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，又因参加一次有多名各地异见人士在福建省厦门市举办的私人聚会（后被当局称为“厦门聚会案”），同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，遂被山东警方从友人家中带走，后被烟台市警方以“厦门聚会案”主犯指定居所监视居住；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，又被临沂市临沭县警方以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，其案被临沂市检察院以颠覆国家政权罪名提起公诉，并移送至临沂市中级法院审判；据悉，密押期间，曾惨遭酷刑折磨，如连续<span lang="EN-US">73 </span>天被剥夺睡眠、连续<span lang="EN-US">8</span>天被“坐老虎凳”（一种极端酷刑）、<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月受只有噪音和<span lang="EN-US">24</span>小时照射日光灯虐待、长期不让洗澡和刷牙、甚至用餐权被剥夺等。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，被中共当局判刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2032</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。目前被羁押于山东省临沭县看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日上午许志永案、丁家喜案二审在临沭县法院第三审判庭宣判：驳回上诉，维持许志永<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年、丁家喜<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年有期徒刑的原判。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日获悉：丁家喜已被转移至湖北江北监狱。</span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/04/12.html<o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/11/blog-post_24.html</span></b></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">丁雪梅：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河南省信阳市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，河南省信阳市法轮功学员陶玉华、杨成云、丁雪梅、白国显、李俊华、杨山萍六人被确山县警察非捕，同时被抢走多部电脑、打印机、真相资料、耗材等物品。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，驻马店驿城区法院宣判。丁雪梅被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; tab-stops: 122.5pt; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">丁燕：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黑龙江哈尔滨香坊区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年年初，哈尔滨疫情严重。<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>、<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，哈尔滨市香坊区<span lang="EN-US">7</span>名法轮功学员李立壮、霍晓辉、唐竹茵、李艳清、丁燕、焦其华、赵丽华，在车上打电话告诉世人大疫来临莫惊慌，诚念“法轮大法好，真善忍好”。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，大庆市让胡路区龙南公安分局在哈尔滨市香坊区抓捕了霍晓辉、李立壮、唐竹茵、丁燕、赵丽华、焦其华、李艳清等<span lang="EN-US">7</span>名法轮功学员，以他们拨打“反宣”电话为名，逮捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，大庆市让胡路区法院在侦查事实不清，证据不足等情况下，枉法对哈尔滨李立壮等<span lang="EN-US">7</span>名法轮功学员下达判决：丁燕被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/3/%E5%93%88%E5%B0%94%E6%BB%A8%E4%B8%83%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%80%E8%87%B3%E5%8D%81%E5%A4%9A%E5%B9%B4-434311.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/3/%E5%93%88%E5%B0%94%E6%BB%A8%E4%B8%83%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%80%E8%87%B3%E5%8D%81%E5%A4%9A%E5%B9%B4-434311.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">丁中福：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">安徽省合肥甘泉教会长老。安徽省合肥甘泉教会教案受害者。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日抓捕的安徽省合肥甘泉教会周松林牧师、丁中福长老、裴德飞传道、茅骏马传道和杨佩云姐妹，被以涉嫌“诈骗罪”刑事拘留，现被羁押在看守所。甘泉教会有二十多年的历史，拥有两处由弟兄姐妹共同购买的房产。目前，这些房产和教会的资金流水都可能成为“诈骗”的证据。一旦罪名成立，这些牧者和同工们将面临极重的判罚。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/12/5_16.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/12/5_16.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">董洪义</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：<span lang="EN-US">1945</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日出生，河北省邯郸市人，河北省邯郸钢铁集团有限责任公司退休工程师，某民营企业管理者，中共党员，中共“<span lang="EN-US">20</span>大”修改党章建议书联署人（之一），民主宪政追求者，中国在押政治犯。自<span lang="EN-US">1983</span>年成为中共党员起，一直关注中共党组织的建设与发展，并认同和主张中共要实行国家民主化管理；近年来，曾因不满习近平主政以来祸国倒行逆施，而在网上经常发一些批评“党和国家领导人，以及一些政府职能部门”等文字，并与同事、友人经常在网上评论国内外政治、经济、社会等形势讯息，遂频遭邯郸当局监控打压，并被数次带走传唤；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，中共“<span lang="EN-US">20</span>大”前期，因现任中共总书记习近平欲在“<span lang="EN-US">20</span>大”召开期间搞个人崇拜，以求长期连任，其遂与另<span lang="EN-US">2</span>位中共老党员（田奇庄和马贵全）拟联名发表建议书，建议“<span lang="EN-US">20</span>大”上修改党章，指称：党章里“党政军民学，东西南北中，党是领导一切的”这种毛式文革用语纯属违宪，应予以删除；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，其等<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人正式发公开信（即建议书）建言献策，呼吁中共修改党章，去除“党领导一切”，禁止任何形式的领导干部搞个人崇拜，杜绝文革历史悲剧的重演；此公开信一经发出，立引社会热议，但同时也使中共河北省当局极为恐慌和不满，三人很快即遭传唤，并被处于严密监控之中；后又因其接受外媒采访，同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，其等先后被邯郸市警方以涉嫌“勾结外国势力”罪由正式刑拘；后其与田奇庄被邯郸市检察院以同罪由正式批捕；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日获悉，其<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人案宗已被邯郸市检察院移交到邯郸市法院，并应于本月庭审；据悉，其家人已帮其找到代理辩护律师，但律师被有关部门告知说“可以走法律程序、参与辩护，但不会起什么作用，具体怎么判，是上面已经定好的”。目前被羁押于邯郸市磁县看守所（河北省邯郸市磁县磁州镇西湖街，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">056500</span>）。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2022</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年底，董洪义先生被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。田奇庄及董洪义均关押在河北省邯郸监狱。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/11/blog-post_13.html"><b><span style="color: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">董立彪：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吉林省榆树市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1959</span>年生，原吉林舒兰市吉舒镇人，曾于<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月被舒兰市公安局警察抓捕构陷，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年。冤狱回家后，他曾被舒兰市吉舒镇警察和不法人员多次骚扰，被迫流落到榆树市。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月董立彪又被警察抓捕、抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月获悉，他被德惠市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，被转监到公主岭监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月。<span class="MsoHyperlink"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; text-decoration: none; text-underline: none;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">董利利：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">江苏省盐城市滨海县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月江号其、董利利和罗云因散发法轮功资料被抓捕到盐城看守所迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年下半年他们都被判刑，江号其被判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，他的未婚妻董利利被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，他的母亲罗云被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，都已被关进监狱。董利利刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山西省临汾金灯台家庭教会同工、基督徒。山西临汾金灯堂教案受害者之一。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，山西临汾金灯堂教会九位负责人和同工被警方抓捕，其中包括曾为信仰坐牢<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年的王晓光牧师和他的妻子、曾为信仰坐牢<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年的杨荣丽姊妹。后来一些同工被取保候审，又有一些新的人被抓捕。现在还在看守所的有<span lang="EN-US">7</span>人<span lang="EN-US">: </span>王晓光牧师及妻子杨荣丽，李双平、董勇勇、赵国爱、霍壮平、吴玲娥。这七人于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被批捕，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被移送检察院审查起诉。据悉，批捕和移送检察院审查起诉的罪名都是涉嫌“诈骗罪”。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/blog-post_39.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/blog-post_39.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">董秀荣<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 11.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">北京法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，北京公安局国保大队及辖下派出所出动大量警力，至少对<span lang="EN-US">31</span>名法轮功学员和两位亲属实施抓捕和抄家。其中包括大兴区法轮功学员刘玉红、刘星、靳淑英、董秀荣<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月获悉，以前的轻判的消息是中共人员欺骗其家人的谎言，实际情况是，刘玉红、刘星、靳淑英均被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月、被罚金五千元，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月。董秀荣被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，被罚金四千元，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/12/46-4.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/12/46-4.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">董瑶琼：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖南泼墨女。董瑶琼<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月初被第三度关进株洲市第三精神病院。长期关注董瑶琼的北京画家华涌是在<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日在推特首先发布了这个消息。而董瑶琼的推特内容基本已经被清空。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月董瑶琼向中共总书记习近平的头像上泼墨，之后被上海公安拘捕，同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日被当局送回老家湖南省株洲市攸县，并以疑有精神病为由，将董瑶琼先后两次关进株洲市医院。董瑶琼在被拘押期间，饱受酷刑虐待。其父董建彪告诉媒体，女儿在关押期间曾被强迫吃药。董瑶琼在获释时，呈现出与原先活泼开朗的样子截然不同的模样。获释后的董瑶琼，变成沉默寡言、神情紧张，甚至是有些痴呆的样子。董瑶琼去年获释后在推特发视频称，当地政府要求她上班，以便于监视。她在视频中强调自己没有精神病，是当局强制把她关入精神病院。后来该推文被删除。目前一直关押在精神病院。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">董怡然：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁沈阳皇姑区法轮功学员。男，<span lang="EN-US">1961</span>年生，家住辽宁省沈阳市皇姑区，原沈阳市公安局刑警支队技术处工程师。<span lang="EN-US">1994</span>年修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年中共迫害法轮功后屡遭迫害，失去工作、被劳教。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，董怡然在发放法轮功资料时，被沈阳市公安局和平区分局马路湾派出所警察抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，董怡然是被关押到沈北新区看守所，因疫情隔离，然后被送沈阳市和平区看守所。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">2022</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，被沈阳市于洪区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，现已被关押在沈阳第<span lang="EN-US">2</span>监狱。监狱方不许他的亲属接见、存钱或物。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/10/29/index.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/10/29/index.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">董郁玉：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1962</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年生，资深评论家、光明日报评论部副主任。<span lang="EN-US">1987</span>年毕业于北京大学法律系，获法学硕士。董郁玉<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>至<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>曾任哈佛大学尼曼研究员、<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年是日本庆应大学的访问学者、<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年是北海道大学公共政策大学院（研究生院）访问教授。董郁玉于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日与一位日本外交官在北京新侨饭店午餐时被中共当局拘捕。后被以“间谍罪”正式逮捕，面临审判。他在中共官媒光明日报工作了<span lang="EN-US">30</span>多年，被抓捕时距离退休还有三个月。<b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/04/blog-post_54.html"><b><span style="color: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/04/blog-post_54.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">窦长营：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江肇东市法轮功学员。窦长营于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日被抓捕、抄家，随即遭刑事拘留、批捕、起诉、判刑。<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日获悉，已经被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2024/01/5_29.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">杜春香：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黑龙江大庆市法轮功学员。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1958</span>年生，大庆市钻井研究所职工，家住大庆市八百垧。<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月修炼法轮功。杜纯香女士因坚持法轮信仰，遭到中共江泽民集团严重迫害，多次遭单位洗脑迫害，曾四次被拘留、两次被判刑，被折磨致双肺结核、高血压，几次吐血，二次被迫害致生活不能自理。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日当天大庆警察抓捕了一百多名法轮功学员，杜春香也被抓捕，被关押在大庆第二看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月获悉，其被被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">。信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/2/6/456491.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast;">石家庄市深泽县法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">1971</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日石家庄市深泽县十多名法轮功学员半夜被突然抓捕，其中杜国防等八人一直被关押在石家庄市第二看守所和晋州市看守所，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日被构陷到晋州市法院，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日在晋州市法院被开庭，据<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日获悉，把人均已被判刑。杜国防被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/6/11/461862.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">杜贺先：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河北雄县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日下午，杜贺先被雄县公安局国保警察抓捕。后杜贺先被保定市中院判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，被从保定看守所转到石家庄女子监狱关押。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">杜景义</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：吉林长春市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年六十多岁，职业是律师，居住在长春市绿园区，一九九六年修炼法轮大。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日上午，杜景义及妻子崔玉秋和女儿一家三人被抓捕。晚上十一点左右，杜的妻子和女儿被放回。杜景义律师于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被长春市朝阳区法院庭审，杜景义为自己作了无罪辩护<span lang="EN-US">.</span>后杜景义律师被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，没有通知家属，上诉被中级法院驳回。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">杜荣：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日下午，杜荣、张珍华、陈世贵正在友人毛坤家做客休息，被成都市金牛区分局国保警察、茶店子派出所孟红等一伙警察疯狂砸门抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，毛坤、杜荣、张珍华、陈世贵被四川省成都市金牛区法院判刑，杜荣判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">天津市法轮功学员，女。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，杜艳红去同修家时被警察抓捕，警察从她背包里搜出了内存卡、法轮功粘贴，当天对其抄家。后杜艳红被取保候审，强制罚金<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月份，法院开庭，杜艳红做了无罪辩护，杜艳红当天回家。后，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月份的一天下午，宁河区芦台镇派出所警察去杜艳红家，让她去派出所一趟办完事就回家，结果杜艳红一去不归，被关押到看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月底，家人这才知道杜艳红被判<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，关押到天津女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/10/13/%E5%A4%A9%E6%B4%A5%E5%B8%82%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E6%9D%9C%E8%89%B3%E7%BA%A2%E8%A2%AB%E5%86%A4%E5%88%A4%E5%8A%AB%E6%8C%81%E5%85%A5%E7%8B%B1-467069.html"><b minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">杜振田：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">山东招远市青年法轮功学员。杜振田一家五口，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日傍晚在不同地点被招远国保抓捕，杜振田一直被关押在异地龙口市。龙口市法院<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月通知律师，对杜振田判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，并罚款<span lang="EN-US">15000</span>元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日止。潍坊监狱因疫情拒收，杜振田现仍被关押在龙口市看守所。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/26/%E5%B1%B1%E4%B8%9C%E6%8B%9B%E8%BF%9C%E5%B8%82%E5%A5%BD%E9%9D%92%E5%B9%B4%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4-440503.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/26/%E5%B1%B1%E4%B8%9C%E6%8B%9B%E8%BF%9C%E5%B8%82%E5%A5%BD%E9%9D%92%E5%B9%B4%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4-440503.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">杜志俊：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">四川省绵阳市江油市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1947</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">75</span>岁。杜志俊、吴启慧夫妇<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被江油市公安局国保大队抄家，抢走电脑和所有大法书籍并被抓捕。杜志俊被抓捕到江油市看守所，吴启慧被抓捕到绵阳市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，杜志俊被江油市法院判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半；吴启慧被江油市法院判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年半。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/6/17/445046.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/6/17/445046.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">段守珍</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：武汉市青山区人，法轮功学员。因信法轮功被长期监控和受到打压迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，当其在武汉市汉口区金家墩邮局附近宣传法轮功时，遭到青山区公安分局郑珂的构陷，随被武汉市汉口区警方刑拘，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月其案件被转至武汉市青山区检察院。期间因证据不足，青山区检察院两次退侦，要求补充资料。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日其案件已转至武汉市青山区法院，武汉市青山区法院于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日庭审，至今刑期未知。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">段宜法：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黑龙江省佳木斯市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1951</span>年生。家住佳木斯市向阳区红旗路北段林机小区红旗佳苑，户籍所在地是佳木斯市郊区。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日上午，佳木斯市向阳公安分局松林派出所片八个警察闯入段宜法家实施抓捕、抄家。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">后被关押在佳木斯市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年末被庭审，后得知段宜法遭判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">多吉扎西（藏）<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">西藏拉萨著名商人、民营企业家、神湖集团创办人多吉扎西于<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年被不公开审判，判处无期徒刑。</b>现西藏自治区法院给多吉扎西定的罪名是“贷款诈骗罪”，然而，该案疑点是，涉案金额仅仅<span lang="EN-US">150</span>万元。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年，北京法律界专家论证结果是，多吉扎西无法认定犯有贷款诈骗罪，仅仅犯挪用资金罪。并建议西藏自治区法院改判有期徒刑。据了解，多吉扎西在狱中坚持不认罪，一直苦苦等待冤案平反，而多吉扎西的哥哥因多次为弟上访，已被西藏维稳部门禁止离开拉萨市。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年多吉扎西的亲人已聘请北京泽博律师事务所的王飞律师为其辩护。王飞前往拉萨后，在多次请求下，终于获得监狱方面探视机会。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">多杰扎才（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">出生不详，西藏那曲地区比如县达塘乡央唐区<span lang="EN-US">4</span>村人，藏族人权捍卫者。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日在拉萨市被拉萨警方拘捕，后被以涉嫌多项罪名正式逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日获知，其被以拉萨市中级法院以“阻止政府在‘纳拉赞巴’圣上开矿”判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，以“私下向他人贷款罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，以“妨碍公务罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，数罪并罚，最终执行有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年。目前被关押在拉萨扎其监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">E.<o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">F.<o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">樊金清</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times lang="EN-US">2023</span>年已<span lang="EN-US">73</span>岁。樊金清女士<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被南岗区公安分局国保大队警察抓捕，一直关押在哈尔滨市第二看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/11/26/%E5%93%88%E5%B0%94%E6%BB%A873%E5%B2%81%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E6%A8%8A%E9%87%91%E6%B8%85%E9%81%AD%E8%AF%AC%E5%88%A4%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-468657.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">樊钧益：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1972</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年出生，湖南省长沙市岳麓区人，网名：<span lang="EN-US">@</span>铁子，推号：<span lang="EN-US">@fanjunyidu</span>，职业不详，多项公益活动组织者及参与者，“中国国民党”忠实粉丝，网络活跃人士，“墙外信息搬运工”，长沙“同城饭醉”活动参与者，民主异见人士，中国在押政治犯。早年，曾组织参与多项公益活动，包括关爱山区学童、定时组织探望敬老院老人及参与公益百公里志愿者活动等，故而深得资助者和维权公民称许和认可；又因其是国军后代，长期坚定支持和拥护三民主义及国民党发到墙内，再由其创建的微信群和<span lang="EN-US">QQ</span>群传发，而屡遭长沙当局打压；曾因按月例行组织并参与“同城饭醉”活动，以及组织经常性的举牌抗议活动等，而被长沙市警方多次“喝茶”、传唤和拘留处罚；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，曾因参与长沙同城公民七月聚餐后举牌声援<span lang="EN-US">709</span>律师和公民，并将举牌照片发到网上，而立遭长沙市岳麓区警方约谈“喝茶”；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，曾因将“美国之音”网站的文图信息转发到微信群组，再次遭岳麓区警方传唤做笔录，其家被查抄；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，曾因举牌要求中共结束一党专政，允许人民在推特发表言论，而被岳麓区警方以“寻衅滋事”罪由行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日<span lang="EN-US">-29</span>日，又因公民聚餐后举牌抗议中共花纳税人的钱举行大阅兵，而被岳麓区警方以“扰乱公共秩序”罪由再次行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，其突然被云南省警方跨省抓捕，次日（<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日）被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘，自此失联；对其被抓，外界曾一度怀疑与“六四”将至，当局恐其会有所动作，以及其近期网络言论和在微信群立转发内容有关，其被持续拘押不放，据悉，其被拘捕更多可能与涉及“武装”、“武装组织”或与此类似的案件有关；迄今，因云南警方拒不答复外界友人对其案情的问询，而其家人又因恐遭警方威胁而选择对外缄默不语，故其更多信息缺详。目前被羁押于云南省昆明市某看守所。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/12/blog-post_14.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/12/blog-post_14.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">范灵秀：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁锦州市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年已年近七十岁。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2022</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，范灵秀被辖区锦州市保安派出所警察抓捕，初期被关押在锦州义县看守所隔离。之后，她被转到锦州市女子看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日得知，范灵秀被锦州市凌海法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。她现仍被关押在锦州市女子看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/1/18/455164.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/1/18/455164.html</span></b></a></span><b
