mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">范美玲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">内蒙古赤峰市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1961</span>年生，现年<span lang="EN-US">62</span>岁，是内蒙古赤峰市宁城县忙农镇三家村一位普通农妇，她因时法轮功学员而频遭当地中共人员骚扰迫害，于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年被迫离家漂泊，近年在河北廊坊居住。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，范美玲在廊坊市安次区租住屋被南门外派出所警察抓捕，关押到廊坊市看守所。随后遭批捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日其被霸州市法院开庭，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并罚金<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元。范美令上诉至廊坊市中级法院，于<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被廊坊市中级法院驳回上诉，维持原判。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/10/16_29.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/10/16_29.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> </span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/10/28/%E5%86%85%E8%92%99%E5%96%84%E8%89%AF%E5%86%9C%E5%A6%87%E8%8C%83%E7%BE%8E%E4%BB%A4%E8%A2%AB%E5%86%A4%E5%88%A4%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-467571.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/10/28/%E5%86%85%E8%92%99%E5%96%84%E8%89%AF%E5%86%9C%E5%A6%87%E8%8C%83%E7%BE%8E%E4%BB%A4%E8%A2%AB%E5%86%A4%E5%88%A4%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-467571.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">范明兰<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吉林省延吉市法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月开始修炼法轮功，因坚持信仰<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年被劳教<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。后被数次抓捕，曾遭酷刑折磨。范明兰<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日左右又被延边州龙井市警察抓捕，七月末家人获悉，她被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">范生汉：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">湖北省十堰市人，公职人员，中共党员，前湖北省十堰市二轻局干部，宜城市信达企业管理咨询合伙企业<span lang="EN-US">(</span>有限合伙<span lang="EN-US">) </span>等股东，湖北襄大集团股份有限公司（以下简称襄大集团）高管、党委书记。<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年代，曾因中共政府在国企改制过程中，被作为湖北省十堰市二轻局干部选派进入襄大集团，故而被襄大集团历聘为下属公司的高管、党务作者及襄大集团党委书记，专门从事协助组建民企党支部、发展党员及规范集团运行等工作；后经其努力，曾发展民企党员<span lang="EN-US">100</span>多名，并将中共党建工作拓展至集团运行的多方面；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年，曾因襄大集团在当地政府动员下斥巨资承债式收购了濒临破产的国企改制化企业（即鄂西化工厂），之后不久，该化工厂即因债权纠纷而引来一场官司；后因襄阳市中级法院就此冻结了该厂的基本账户，致使该化工厂职工养老金停发、社保停缴，遂为生计，近<span lang="EN-US">800</span>名职工开始集体上访维权；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，其与襄大集团董事长张武德、总经理张国祥等<span lang="EN-US">10</span>名高管突然被十堰市竹溪县警方以涉嫌“聚众冲击国家机关罪”带走、刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，又被以“带领职工冲击法院”和“高利转贷”为由，被十堰市竹溪县检察院以涉嫌“组织、领导、参加黑社会性质组织罪”及“强迫交易、聚众冲击国家机关、寻衅滋事”等八罪起诉；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，其等多人案在法院开庭审理时，“组织、领导黑社会性质组织”等罪名终被取消，但仍将被湖北省十堰市竹溪县法院以“寻衅滋事罪、拘禁罪、串通投标罪、高利转贷罪、聚众冲击国家机关罪”五罪予以重判；据悉，同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，因其妻突然接到看守所通知，要求其等家属尽快为其办理取保候审手续且不能提前相见，遂被其妻断然拒绝，后其妻到湖北省信访局投诉，并网发求助信呼吁关注，人们才知其在竹溪看守所超期关押近<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，经常遭酷刑折磨，现已“被关昏迷、右半身瘫痪，被送进医院重症监护室”；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日又悉，又有涉案人员家属<span lang="EN-US">12</span>人（含其妻向玉香）联合发出控告信，披露竹溪县办案机关长时间使用刑讯逼供、威胁和诱供等手段，取证等事实；后其等一行多人案经几次重审，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，终被湖北省十堰市竹溪县法院以“寻衅滋事罪、拘禁罪、串通投标罪、高利转贷罪、聚众冲击国家机关罪”统一宣判，现除已知襄大集团董事长张德武被重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年，其余人等刑期均不明晰，但知均对判决表示不服，将会提起上诉。目前被羁押于十堰市竹溪县看守所。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/02/blog-post_63.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/02/blog-post_63.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">范伟：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁本溪市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1958</span>年生。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月份，开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，到西湖区彩北派出所，跟警察讲法轮功，结果，范伟被警察抓捕，后又被转至本溪市看守所关押。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，他被本溪市南芬区法院视频开庭，并判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/2/%E4%BF%AE%E7%82%BC%E5%A4%A7%E6%B3%95%E4%BB%85%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4-%E8%BE%BD%E5%AE%81%E6%9C%AC%E6%BA%AA%E5%B8%8263%E5%B2%81%E8%8C%83%E4%BC%9F%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4-434263.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/2/%E4%BF%AE%E7%82%BC%E5%A4%A7%E6%B3%95%E4%BB%85%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4-%E8%BE%BD%E5%AE%81%E6%9C%AC%E6%BA%AA%E5%B8%8263%E5%B2%81%E8%8C%83%E4%BC%9F%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4-434263.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">范文成：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广东省广州市常居人口，原广州市某房地产中介商，广州<span lang="EN-US">11</span>·<span lang="EN-US">12</span>大抓捕受害人，民主异见人士，中国在押政治犯。近年来，虽经常参与民主维权活动及与民主友人在一起的聚餐活动，但因其为人处事低调，故而一直鲜为人知；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，当其与民主友人胡天峰为谋生计正忙于筹备合伙成立一所保安公司之时，突然与民主公民范一平、胡天峰等多人被广东省广州市国安局以“颠覆国家政权”为由抓捕，并被指定居所监视居住；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，又被以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”转刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，知其被以涉嫌同罪名正式逮捕，另有范一平等<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人亦被同期转正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，知其五人案被移送至广州市检察院审查起诉；之后，又于同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，案宗被移送至广州市中级法院，五人均被以“颠覆国家政权罪”起诉，案由涉及组党，具体事实无非聚餐闲聊时政、去云南旅游等；<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，其被认定为主犯终被广州市中级法院以“颠覆国家政权罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2032</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。目前被羁押于广州市安全局看守所（广州市花都区迎宾大道<span lang="EN-US">111</span>号，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">510800</span>）。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/08/121112.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/08/121112.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">范学斌：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁省营口市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1973</span>年出生的范学斌，因坚持法轮功信仰，两次被中共法院判刑八年，一次是<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，范学斌刑满出狱仅一年五个月，就又遭警察绑架。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年其又遭抓捕，随即又被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年。在狱中其遭酷刑虐待，以至于现在双腿也不能站立行走。范学斌现被关押在辽宁省大连监狱，距结束冤刑还有八个月，据悉，范学斌已被监狱迫害致不能行走，须用轮椅代步。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/10/8_16.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/10/8_16.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/10/16/%E5%86%A4%E5%88%91%E5%85%AB%E5%B9%B4%E5%8F%88%E5%85%AB%E5%B9%B4-%E8%8C%83%E5%AD%A6%E6%96%8C%E8%A2%AB%E5%A4%A7%E8%BF%9E%E7%9B%91%E7%8B%B1%E8%BF%AB%E5%AE%B3%E8%87%B4%E6%AE%8B-467169.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/10/16/%E5%86%A4%E5%88%91%E5%85%AB%E5%B9%B4%E5%8F%88%E5%85%AB%E5%B9%B4-%E8%8C%83%E5%AD%A6%E6%96%8C%E8%A2%AB%E5%A4%A7%E8%BF%9E%E7%9B%91%E7%8B%B1%E8%BF%AB%E5%AE%B3%E8%87%B4%E6%AE%8B-467169.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">范一平：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1950</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年代生，广东省广州市人，中共干部家庭出身，曾就读于军医大学，毕业后任外科医生，后转行成为某食品贸易公司经营者，成功珠宝商，自民主墙以来的老民运，中国在押政治犯。自民主墙时期就参与民主运动，多年来一直致力于推动中国社会的人权及法治进步事业，故长期受到当局监控和敏感时期被限制人身自由；<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年末，曾因接待秘密回国推动民主运动的中国异议人士王炳章，并帮助另一位异见人士王希哲逃往美国，而被中共广东当局判刑入狱三年；出狱后，因继续持守民主理念和抗争，<span lang="EN-US"> 2014</span>年六四前夕，曾再次被广州警方以“寻衅滋事” 为由行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天，其居所遭搜查；因中共最高领导人习近平主政以来，对民主异见人士监控、打压愈加强烈，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，其与另四名民运人士范文成、赖见君、乔连红、韦亚妮在“广州<span lang="EN-US">11</span>·<span lang="EN-US">12</span>大抓捕”中，被广州市警方先后以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”抄家后带走；次日，其被送进医院，而后被指定居所监视住；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，除乔连红被取保释放之外，其与接续被抓捕的赖天龙及范文成、胡天峰等<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人均被广州市国家安全局以同罪名正式批捕；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，其一行<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人案被当地警方移交至广州市检察院审查起诉，<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，其案件又被移送到广州市中级法院；<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人均被以“颠覆国家政权罪”起诉，案由涉及组党，具体事实多为聚餐闲聊时政、去云南旅游等；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，其<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人案被广州市检察院移交至广州市中级法院；<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，终被广州市中级法院以“颠覆国家政权罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。目前被羁押于广州巿花都看守所（广东省广州市花都区新华镇宝华路<span lang="EN-US">32</span>号，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">510899</span>）。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/06/11124.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/06/11124.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">范志勇：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东省东营市胜利油田河口区法轮功学员。范志勇、孙玉霞法轮功夫妇于<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年七月曾因制作发放神韵光盘，被山东滨州沾化法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，孙玉霞被判缓刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。范志勇于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年出狱后，被单位开除，失去了生活经济来源，为了生活和孙玉霞走到一起，开办“小饭桌”维持生计。范志勇、孙玉霞夫妇<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日被警察被抓捕，日前被东营区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚款两万元；孙玉霞被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万六千元。范志勇刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/1/8/454651.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/1/8/454651.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">方世梅：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">云南省文山州法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年生，原文山州烟草公司职工。一九九七年，方世梅开始修炼法轮功，自中共一九九九年七月开始迫害法轮功后，方世梅多次遭迫害，曾三次被绑架到“洗脑班”，二零零四年被非法判刑五年。在云南省第二女子监狱，她多次被关禁闭室，累计一年之久，还曾被偷偷下药，致她生命垂危。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2022</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日上午，方世梅和廖文仙在文山州西畴县马街发放法轮功资料时，被监控摄像拍到，后方世梅、廖文仙被抓捕抄家。方世梅和廖文仙被关押在西畴县看守所，后被构陷到法院，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月获悉她们分别被判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年、<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2032</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.5pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/11/10.html"><b </span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/11/23/%E4%BA%91%E5%8D%97%E6%96%B9%E4%B8%96%E6%A2%85%E3%80%81%E5%BB%96%E6%96%87%E4%BB%99%E5%88%86%E5%88%AB%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E5%8D%81%E5%B9%B4%E3%80%81%E4%B8%83%E5%B9%B4-468535.html</span></b></a></span><b Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">方宗菊：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1961</span>年生，湖北孝感市安陆市法轮功学员。因修炼法轮功方宗菊曾经被判刑两年。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，方宗菊在安陆市区讲法轮功被抓捕，被抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被安陆市法院庭审，多日后得知她被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">冯立齐：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吉林农安县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，长春市农安县抓捕了<span lang="EN-US">20</span>多名法轮功学员。此次抓捕行动，是由长春市政法委和农安县政法委共同策划实施的。此次被抓捕的法轮功学员有</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">张秀芝、高晓歧、蔡玉英、吴冬梅、于姣茹、单为和、赵秀兰、孙秀英、张敬元、冯立齐、吕相富、董秀辉等<span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">22</span><span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">名法轮功学员被抓捕。他们被抓捕、构陷<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多后，有十几名法轮功学员被德惠市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>至<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年。其中：</span>冯立齐<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">被判<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/5/%E5%90%89%E6%9E%9713%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%BA%8C%E5%88%B0%E5%8D%81%E5%B9%B4-%E4%B8%AD%E6%B3%95%E7%BB%B4%E6%8C%81%E5%86%A4%E5%88%A4-434381.html"><b mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">冯莲霞</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：黑龙江大庆法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1957</span>年生，大庆油田物资装备总公司供应公司采油五厂器材站退休职工，家住采油四厂晨曦小区。一九九八年，冯莲霞开始修炼法轮功。在二十多年来，冯莲霞只因坚持法轮功信仰，曾遭中共多次抓捕、劳教及经济迫害，曾遭酷刑折磨。冯莲霞<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，被红岗区公安分局警察抓捕，被铐在铁椅子上八、九个小时后以“取保候审”回家。此后，公检法继续司法构陷她。同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，冯莲霞再次被抓捕。一年后，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月获悉，冯莲霞被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，被关押至黑龙江省女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">。</b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/09/3_24.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/9/14/%E5%B1%A1%E9%81%AD%E5%8A%B3%E6%95%99%E3%80%81%E5%85%B3%E6%8A%BC%E6%8A%98%E7%A3%A8-%E5%A4%A7%E5%BA%86%E5%86%AF%E8%8E%B2%E9%9C%9E%E5%86%8D%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E5%85%A5%E7%8B%B1-465295.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">冯瑞英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁省建平县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1972</span>年生。家住辽宁省朝阳市建平县奎德素镇北山村六组。冯瑞英于一九九七年十一月开始修炼法轮功。自中共一九九九年七月开始公开迫害法轮功后，冯瑞英遭到绑架、关押等多次迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日在家中被建平县警察抓捕；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日遭建平县法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元。后被押入到马三家监狱迫害。刑期到：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/7/27/2022-7-27.html#22726231132-10"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/7/27/2022-7-27.html#22726231132-10</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">冯少勇：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1971</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月出生，湖北省仙桃市张沟镇人，北京邮电大学博士，前北京邮电大学，广东省深圳市龙岗区长住居民，原深圳市某中学员工，法轮功信仰者，中国在押良心犯。早年曾在北京邮电大学读博士生，为人乐观谦和，人缘好，因是研究项目组技术骨干，曾于<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年在该校与同事成功研发机顶盒，并将个人所获奖金<span lang="EN-US">100</span>万全部捐给该校；但因信仰、宣传法轮功，遭中共北京当局严厉打压；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，其被深圳市龙岗区警方突然抓捕，次日被刑事拘留，并被送深圳市龙岗区看守所关押，其所在中学办公室、宿舍，其家及亲戚家当天均被查抄；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，被以涉嫌“邪教罪”转正式逮捕，控其与另一法轮功友人陈泽奇“均系法轮功组织成员，二人利用掌握的专业知识，组装伪基站给他人，并使用伪基站宣传法轮功”，属于违法行为；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，其案件被深圳市龙岗区法院开庭受理，至<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，其被深圳市龙岗法院一审以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，并罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；其不服上诉，同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日经深圳市中级人民法院终审裁定，驳回上诉、维持原判，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。目前在广东省四会监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">冯小妹：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">江苏无锡市滨湖区拆迁受害者冯小妹，因被起诉于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日再次被无锡市滨湖区人民法院以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”批准逮捕，现羁押在无锡市第二看守所。冯小妹因房屋拆迁和家中财物被抢等问题，在当地始终无法解决，遂于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日到北京天安门裸奔维权，被当地公安人员带回后以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘。在被非法羁押<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月后，于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被无锡市公安局滨湖分局批准逮捕，在关押期间，冯小妹被两次强迫做精神病鉴定，其家人多次前往交涉无果，之后因为滨湖区雪浪街道要跟冯小妹谈拆迁问题，于是在<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日将她取保候审释放回家。在取保期间，冯小妹并未进京上访维权，却于<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日又被滨湖区法院以同样罪名批准逮捕关押。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日开庭。后判决讯息全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">冯颖军：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">北京朝阳区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月底，被海淀区清河派出所警察抓捕，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月底。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/26/446805.html#22725222336-9"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/26/446805.html#22725222336-9</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">冯勇军：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1973</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日出生，四川省绵阳市三台县人，原三台县百顷镇黄龙村二组<span lang="EN-US">023</span>号村民，现成都市金牛区金周路长住居民，实名举报人，人称“锦旗哥”，维权公民，中国在押维权人士。因冯勇军平素为人品行正直，凡其村中所遇不公之事均敢直言，以维护自己及村民的权益，故而颇得村民好评和认可，但却被村领导视为极好管闲事者而颇遭忌恨和报复性打压；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日<span lang="EN-US">-11</span>日，曾因对村中外包养鱼的百顷水库被严重污染而不满，并就申请村里水库承包合同公开、水库资金流向等问题向当地政府提起多项行政诉讼以寻求救济而无果，而与<span lang="EN-US">9</span>位村民联合给三台县环保局和三台县百顷镇党委政府各送一面“不作为”锦旗，以示警示，遂被三台县警方以涉嫌“扰乱社会秩序罪”刑拘，并送三台县看守所关押；获释后，又因不服当地警方处罚决定，而曾实名举报三台县公安局<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日处置送“不作为”锦旗事件违法违规，以期公安部及四川省公安厅指令绵阳市警方调查处理，但结局却是绵阳市警方以情况汇报系工作秘密、国家机密、国家绝密为由而拒不告知；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日<span lang="EN-US">-2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，曾因多次举报被警方非法限制人身自由和成都市青羊区警方行政不作为，并向青羊区法院提起诉讼，而被该法院以“属于刑事案件，不属于人民法院审查范围”为由作出多份行政裁定书，不予受理；后其被逼无奈，就多次持续报警并通过新浪微博声讨青羊区警方的不作为，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，遂被成都市青羊区警方以“扰乱单位秩序”为由处行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">14</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，因冯勇军第<span lang="EN-US">10</span>次来到四川高院蜀汉路办公区据悉投诉维权，而被成都市郫都区警方再次扣押，后被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，被成都市郫都区检察院以同罪名正式批捕；据悉，其已给其妻子亲笔留言要求帮请律师。目前被羁押于成都市新都区看守所（四川省成都市新都区鸿运大道西端<span lang="EN-US">800</span>号，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">610500</span>）。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/09/blog-post_11.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/09/blog-post_11.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">冯蕴青：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">武汉法轮功学员。冯蕴青于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被绑架，关押在武汉东西湖区武汉第一看守所。参与绑架和扣押的部门有：武汉市网监支队，武汉市“国保”支队，江岸区公安分局后湖派出所。冯蕴青于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月被武汉市汉阳区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，冯蕴青不服判决，上诉到武汉市法院，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月武汉中级法院二审维持原判。现在冯蕴青被非法关押在武汉女子监狱（位于武汉市宝丰路）。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">丰晓燕：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">毕业于山东师范大学新闻系，临沂市人大副调研员，副县级。二十多年公职期间因不满现有体制不被提拔，不允出国，不准考取研究生博士职称学历，<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年被市政府组织黑社会撞断腰，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年春天退党退公职，单位拒绝。同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月公开支持香港反送中，被送进派出所拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年新冠疫情间对体制内失察渎职，捐款贪污，罔顾人命，胡作非为忍无可忍，故上京发声。却被侮辱为精神病并强制治疗。丰晓燕拒不认罪，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日被送至临沂第四精神病院，北京路育才路派出所二十多位警察，将患有腰椎间盘突出的丰晓燕在水泥地板拖行至住院部三楼，未进行精神检测，强行关进精神病医院。污蔑其为精神分裂症并强制用药。一直关押在精神病医院。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">付常国：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"> 1985</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日出生，广东省深圳市人，“打工者中心劳动力”（<span lang="EN-US">Worker Empowerment</span>）工作人员，劳动法律咨询者，公益维权者，中国在押维权人士。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">自<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年始，其所在打工者中心以开展公益事业为己任，每年为至少<span lang="EN-US">500</span>名企业外来打工者提供免费法律咨询，举办超过<span lang="EN-US">200</span>余次免费文娱学习活动，使至少十万名工友受惠，因其亦参与其中，遂倍受基层工友的广泛欢迎；自<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年以来，因焊接设备制造商深圳佳士科技<span lang="EN-US">(Jasic Technology)</span>与员工发生劳资冲突，佳士员工愤起维权抗议，其代表“打工者中心”前往调查介入，并与另<span lang="EN-US">3</span>名佳士工友积极尝试在中国大陆组建工会（类似于欧美国家里专门为工人谋福利的“工会”，而非“中华全国总工会”），遂遭到当局的严厉打击，被深圳警方多次传唤；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，参与组建工会的<span lang="EN-US">3</span>名工人因“试图成立非法工会”而被警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”拘押，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，其因在警察局门外喊口号声援被抓工人，故而亦被深圳市坪山区警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，又被以涉嫌“聚众扰乱社会秩序罪”正式逮捕；据悉，其姐付红娥曾于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日为其递交“取保候审申请书”遭拒，理由是一旦批准申请，就“可能毁灭、伪造证据，干扰证人作证或者串供”，<span lang="EN-US">2019 </span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US"> 1</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日又在深圳市第二看守所给其汇款后被“查无此人”退回，迄今不予释放。目前被羁押于深圳市第二看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">付娟：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">西安丰盛基督教教会传道、财务。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日西安市十里铺派出所以“诈骗罪”为由将西安丰盛教会的廉长年牧师、廉旭亮牧师和付娟抓捕，三人都被执行指定居所监视居住。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，被指定居所监视居住长达半年之久的西安丰盛教会的廉长年牧师、廉旭亮牧师、付娟传道被以涉嫌诈骗罪的名义刑事拘留，羁押到看守所。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2023</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日上午，廉长年牧师、廉旭亮牧师、付娟传道的代理律师获准分别会见了当事人。据他们三人的口述，在指定监视居住期间，他们都受到不同程度的虐待和刑讯逼供。审讯人员用廉长年牧师的儿子廉旭亮牧师来威胁他，并且共有七八次殴打廉旭亮牧师，甚至当着廉长年的牧师的面殴打。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/02/blog-post_39.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/02/blog-post_39.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp;</span></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/02/blog-post_18.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/02/blog-post_18.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; tab-stops: 122.5pt; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">付淑贤：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黑龙江哈尔滨平房区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月获悉，付淑贤被开庭时不让与家人见面，已被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，现身体状况不正常，不能行走。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<u><span lang="EN-US">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/3/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E4%B8%89%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-436376.html</span></u></b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">傅炫娟：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">深圳销售圣经播放器案被捕人员之一。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1978</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日出生，汉族，中专学历，原籍地是广西壮族自治区北海市合浦县常乐镇大教村；</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">深圳市生命树文化传播有限公司是一家成立于<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月的合法企业。因销售圣经播放器，竟然导致傅炫娟、邓天永、韩丽、冯群豪等四基督徒被逮捕。中共当局于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，以所谓非法经营罪将他们抓走，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月遭正式逮捕。目前傅炫娟、邓天永、韩丽、冯群豪等</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">4</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">位基督徒都被关押在深圳九围看守所。其家人和律师都被威胁，不得透露案情。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2021</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，宝安区法院认定傅炫娟、邓天永、韩丽、冯群豪等四基督徒犯“非法经营罪”，宣判：傅炫娟有期徒刑六年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">20</span>万元；邓天永三年有期徒刑，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元；冯群豪两年六个月有期徒刑，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元；韩丽一年零三个月有期徒刑，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；另外没收六种型号播放机、电脑主机<span lang="EN-US">2</span>台；其它电脑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>台。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">付燕飞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">长春法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1976</span>年生，毕业于东北师范大学生命科学学院本科，是高中教师，于<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>年毕业前夕开始修炼法轮功，因修炼法轮功曾被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日晚，付燕飞因在劳动公园讲真相，被受中共谎言毒害的人诬告，后被和顺街派出所抓捕，被朝阳区检察院批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年元月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，付燕飞被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">付曌翠</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">:1968</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年生，原是海林市中医院护士长。在中共自<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年对法轮功二十四年的迫害中，她因坚持法轮功信仰，多次遭中共迫害，两次被判刑——<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，付曌翠和母亲汤玉华遭法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，被关押到哈尔滨女子监狱迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，付曌翠被牡丹江铁路公安处劳教<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，因身体检查不合格，哈尔滨戒毒所不收，付曌翠又被送回牡丹江铁路看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，付曌翠以监外执行的形式回到家中。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，付曌翠又被海林国保警察抓捕，后以“取保候审”形式回家。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月末，付曌萃被海林市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并罚金一万元。她上诉到牡丹江市中级法院。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，付曌翠被海林市国保警察和法院抓捕到牡丹江医学院附属二院（俗称公安医院，门前挂着牡丹江看守所的牌子）。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，警察将她从牡丹江市医学院附属二院劫持到牡丹江看守所，之后又被关押到黑龙江省女子监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2030</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/09/96.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/09/96.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/8/31/%E9%81%AD%E8%AF%AC%E5%88%A4%E4%B9%9D%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-%E9%BB%91%E9%BE%99%E6%B1%9F%E4%BB%98%E6%9B%8C%E7%BF%A0%E5%A5%B3%E5%A3%AB%E8%A2%AB%E5%8A%AB%E6%8C%81%E5%85%A5%E7%8B%B1-464770.html</span></b></a></span><b
